# Surah 13 — Ar-Rad

**Status:** ✅ Publishable · Fidelity 100/100 · Prose overlap (4-gram) 0.061 · Longest prose run 15 words · Em dashes 0

**Overlap spans to check:** "it will be said to the jews on the day of resurrection what do you"

---

## 13:1 — verse 1

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat al-Ra'd

[It is Meccan]

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

As for the discussion of the disjointed letters at the beginnings of the surahs, it has already been presented at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah. We stated there that every surah that begins with these letters contains a vindication of the Qur'an and a clarification that its revelation from Allah is true, with no doubt, no uncertainty, and no suspicion about it. This is why He said: {Those are the verses of the Book}, meaning: these are the verses of the Book, which is the Qur'an. It has also been said that it refers to the Torah and the Gospel, as stated by Mujahid and Qatadah, but this view is questionable, indeed far-fetched.

Then He connected to this, by way of joining descriptions, His statement: {And that which has been sent down to you}, meaning: O Muhammad, {from your Lord is the truth}. This is a predicate whose subject has preceded it, namely His statement {And that which has been sent down to you from your Lord}. This is the correct view, and it corresponds to the interpretation of Mujahid and Qatadah. Ibn Jarir preferred that the "wa" (and) be considered redundant, or that it join one description to another description, as we mentioned before, and he cited as evidence the poet's line:

"To the courageous king, and the son of the resolute one, and the lion of the battalion in the throng."

His statement: {But most of the people do not believe} is like His statement: {And most of the people, even if you desire it eagerly, will not be believers} [Yusuf: 103], meaning: despite this clarity, explication, and clearness, most of them do not believe, because of the discord, obstinacy, and hypocrisy present within them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الرَّعْدِ

[وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ] 

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

أَمَّا الْكَلَامُ عَلَى الْحُرُوفُ الْمُقَطَّعَةُ فِي أَوَائِلِ السُّوَرِ، فَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ، وقَدَّمنا أَنَّ كُلَّ سُورَةٍ تَبتدأ بِهَذِهِ الْحُرُوفِ فَفِيهَا الِانْتِصَارُ لِلْقُرْآنِ، وَتِبْيَانُ أَنْ نُزُولَهُ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ حَقٌّ لَا شَكَّ فِيهِ وَلَا مِرْيَةَ وَلَا رَيْبَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿تِلْكَ آيَاتُ الْكِتَابِ﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ آيَاتُ الْكِتَابِ، وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ، وَقِيلَ: التَّوْارَةُ وَالْإِنْجِيلُ. قَالَهُ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ، وَفِيهِ نَظَرٌ بَلْ هُوَ بَعِيدٌ.

ثُمَّ عَطَفَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ عَطْفَ صِفَاتٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِي أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ﴿مِنْ رَبِّكَ الْحَقُّ﴾ خَبَرٌ تَقَدَّمُ مُبْتَدَؤُهُ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِي أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الصَّحِيحُ الْمُطَابِقُ لِتَفْسِيرِ مُجَاهِدٍ وَقَتَادَةَ. وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنْ تَكُونَ الْوَاوُ زَائِدَةً أَوْ عَاطِفَةً صِفَةً عَلَى صِفَةٍ كَمَا قَدَّمْنَا، وَاسْتَشْهَدَ بِقَوْلِ الشَّاعِرُ:

إِلَى المَلك القَرْمِ وَابْنِ الهُمَام ... وَلَيث الْكَتِيبَةِ فِي المُزْدَحَمْ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ وَلَوْ حَرَصْتَ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٠٣] أَيْ: مَعَ هَذَا الْبَيَانِ وَالْجَلَاءِ وَالْوُضُوحِ، لَا يُؤْمِنُ أَكْثَرُهُمْ لِمَا فِيهِمْ مِنَ الشِّقَاقِ وَالْعِنَادِ وَالنِّفَاقِ.

---

## 13:2 — verse 2

### Translation

God Almighty informs us of the completeness of His power and the greatness of His dominion: that it is He who, by His permission and command, raised the heavens without pillars. Rather, by His permission, command, and subjugation, He raised them above the earth to a distance that cannot be attained and whose extent cannot be grasped. The lowest heaven encompasses the entire earth and all that surrounds it of water and air, from all its sides, directions, and regions, elevated above it equally from every side. The distance between it and the earth on every side is a journey of five hundred years, and its own thickness is a journey of five hundred years. Then the second heaven encompasses the lowest heaven and all it contains, and the distance between the two is a journey of five hundred years, and its thickness is five hundred years. Then the third heaven encompasses the second, with what is in it, and the distance between the two is five hundred years, and its thickness is five hundred years. So it is with the fourth, fifth, sixth, and seventh, as [God] Almighty said: {God is He who created seven heavens and of the earth their like. The command descends between them so that you may know that God has power over all things and that God encompasses all things in knowledge} [al-Talaq: 12]. And in the hadith: "The seven heavens and what is in them and what is between them are, in comparison to the Kursi (footstool), like a ring thrown down in a vast desert, and the Kursi in comparison to the Throne is like that ring in that desert." And in another version: "and the Throne, none can measure its measure except God, Mighty and Exalted." It has been reported from some of the predecessors that the distance between the Throne and the earth is a journey of fifty thousand years, and the distance between its two sides is a journey of fifty thousand years, and it is made of red ruby.

As for His saying {without pillars that you can see}, it is reported from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, al-Hasan, and Qatadah that they said: it has pillars, but they cannot be seen.

Iyas ibn Muawiyah said: the heaven is above the earth like a dome, meaning without pillars. The same has been reported from Qatadah, and this is what best fits the context. What is apparent from His saying {and He holds back the heaven from falling upon the earth except by His permission} [al-Hajj: 65] supports this. Accordingly, His saying {that you can see} would be an emphasis negating that, meaning: it is raised without pillars, as you can see it. This is the most perfect expression of power. And in the poetry of Umayyah ibn Abi al-Salt, whose poetry believed while his heart disbelieved, as reported in the hadith, and which is also attributed to Zayd ibn Amr ibn Nufayl, may God have mercy on him and be pleased with him:

"And You are He who, out of favor, grace, and mercy, sent to Moses a messenger calling out...

So I said to him: go, you and Aaron, and call to God Pharaoh, who was a tyrant...

And say to him: did you level this without a peg, until it settled as it is?

And say to him: did you raise this without pillars? Be gentle then, You who built it.

And say to him: did you make its middle luminous, a guide when the night covers you in darkness?

And say to him: who sends forth the sun in the morning, so that whatever of the earth it touches becomes bright?

And say to him: who causes the seed to sprout in the moist earth, so that the plant grows from it, swaying upon a hillock?

And brings forth from it its grain in its heads. In that are signs for one who is attentive."

As for His saying {then He established Himself above the Throne}, its interpretation was given previously in Surat al-Araf, and it is to be passed over as it has come, without specifying a modality, without likening it to anything, without denying it, and without drawing an analogy. Exalted is God, greatly exalted above that.

As for His saying {and He subjected the sun and the moon, each running for an appointed term}, it is said that the meaning is that the two run until their cessation with the establishment of the Hour, as in His saying {and the sun runs to its resting place, that is the determination of the Almighty, the All-Knowing} [Ya-Sin: 38].

And it is said that the meaning is until their resting place, which is beneath the Throne, on the side facing the interior of the earth from the other direction. For they, and the rest of the stars, when they reach there, are at their farthest point from the Throne. Because the Throne, according to the correct view supported by the evidence, is a dome overlooking the world from this direction, and it is not encompassing like the other celestial spheres, because it has legs and bearers who carry it. This cannot be conceived of in a spherical celestial sphere. This is clear to whoever reflects upon what has come in the verses and authentic hadiths. To God belongs praise and grace.

He mentioned the sun and the moon specifically because they are the most manifest of the seven wandering stars (planets), which are the noblest and greatest among the fixed stars. If He has subjected these, then it follows all the more surely and rightly that the rest of the stars are included in this subjugation, as He indicated by His saying {do not prostrate to the sun nor to the moon, but prostrate to God who created them, if it is Him you worship} [Fussilat: 37], along with His explicit statement in {and the sun and the moon and the stars are made subservient by His command. Indeed to Him belong creation and command. Blessed is God, Lord of the worlds} [al-Araf: 54].

As for His saying {He details the signs so that you may be certain of meeting your Lord}, meaning: He makes clear the signs and the proofs that indicate that there is no god but Him, and that He will bring creation back into being when He wills, just as He originated its creation.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى عَنْ كَمَالِ قُدْرَتِهِ وَعَظِيمِ سُلْطَانِهِ: أَنَّهُ الَّذِي بِإِذْنِهِ وَأَمْرِهِ رَفَع السَّمَاوَاتِ بِغَيْرِ عمَد، بَلْ بِإِذْنِهِ وَأَمْرِهِ وَتَسْخِيرِهِ رَفَعَهَا عَنِ الْأَرْضِ بُعدًا لَا تُنَالُ ولا يدرك مداها، فالسماء الدنيا محيطة بِجَمِيعِ الْأَرْضِ وَمَا حَوْلَهَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ وَالْهَوَاءِ مِنْ جَمِيعِ نَوَاحِيهَا وَجِهَاتِهَا وَأَرْجَائِهَا، مُرْتَفِعَةٌ عَلَيْهَا مِنْ كُلِّ جَانِبٍ عَلَى السَّوَاءِ، وَبُعْدُ مَا بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَ الْأَرْضِ مِنْ كُلِّ نَاحِيَةِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسمِائَةِ عَامِ، وَسُمْكُهَا فِي نَفْسِهَا مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسمِائَةِ عَامٍ. ثُمَّ السَّمَاءُ الثَّانِيَةُ مُحِيطَةٌ بِالسَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَمَا حَوَتْ، وَبَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَهَا مِنَ الْبُعْدِ مَسِيرَةُ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَسُمْكُهَا خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، ثُمَّ السَّمَاءُ الثَّالِثَةُ مُحِيطَةٌ بِالثَّانِيَةِ، بِمَا فِيهَا، وَبَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَهَا خَمْسُمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَسُمْكُهَا خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ، وَكَذَا الرَّابِعَةُ وَالْخَامِسَةُ وَالسَّادِسَةُ وَالسَّابِعَةُ، كَمَا قَالَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَ سَبْعَ سَمَاوَاتٍ وَمِنَ الأرْضِ مِثْلَهُنَّ يَتَنزلُ الأمْرُ بَيْنَهُنَّ لِتَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَحَاطَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا﴾ [الطَّلَاقِ: ١٢] وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "مَا السماواتُ السَّبْعُ وَمَا فِيهِنَّ وَمَا بَيْنَهُنَّ فِي الْكُرْسِيِّ إِلَّا كَحَلْقَةٍ مُلْقَاةٍ بِأَرْضِ فَلاة، وَالْكُرْسِيِّ فِي الْعَرْشِ كَتِلْكَ الْحَلْقَةِ فِي تِلْكَ الْفَلَاةِ وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "وَالْعَرْشُ لَا يُقَدِّرُ قَدْرَهُ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَجَاءَ عَنْ بَعْضِ السَّلَفِ أَنَّ بُعْدَ مَا بَيْنَ الْعَرْشِ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ مَسِيرَةَ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ، وَبُعْدَ مَا بَيْنَ قُطْرَيْهِ مَسِيرَةَ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ، وَهُوَ مِنْ يَاقُوتَةٍ حَمْرَاءَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بِغَيْرِ عَمَدٍ تَرَوْنَهَا﴾ رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَقَتَادَةَ: أَنَّهُمْ: قَالُوا: لَهَا عَمَد وَلَكِنْ لَا تُرَى.

وَقَالَ إِيَاسُ بْنُ مُعَاوِيَةَ: السَّمَاءُ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ مِثْلُ الْقُبَّةِ، يَعْنِي بِلَا عَمَدٍ. وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، وَهَذَا هُوَ اللَّائِقُ بِالسِّيَاقِ. وَالظَّاهِرُ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيُمْسِكُ السَّمَاءَ أَنْ تَقَعَ عَلَى الأرْضِ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٦٥] فَعَلَى هَذَا يَكُونُ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَرَوْنَهَا﴾ تَأْكِيدًا لِنَفْي ذَلِكَ، أَيْ: هِيَ مَرْفُوعَةٌ بِغَيْرِ عَمْدٍ كَمَا تَرَوْنَهَا. هَذَا هُوَ الْأَكْمَلُ فِي الْقُدْرَةِ. وَفِي شِعْرِ أُمَيَّةَ بْنِ أَبِي الصَّلْتِ الَّذِي آمَنَ شِعْرُهُ وَكَفَرَ قَلْبُهُ، كَمَا وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ وَيُرْوَى لِزَيْدِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ نُفَيْلٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ وَرَضِيَ عَنْهُ:

وأنتَ الَّذِي مِنْ فَضْل مَنٍّ وَرَحْمَة ... بَعَثتَ إلى مُوسَى رَسُولا مُنَاديا ...

فقلت له: فاذهَبْ وهارونَ فادعُوَا ... إِلَى اللَّهِ فرْعَونَ الَّذِي كانَ طَاغيا ...

وَقُولا لَهُ: هَلْ أنتَ سَوّيت هَذه ... بِلَا [وتَد حَتَّى اطْمَأَنَّتْ كَمَا هِيَا

وقُولا له: أأنتَ رَفَّعتَ هَذه ... بلا] عَمَد أرْفِقْ إذَا بَِك بانيَا؟ ...

وَقُولا لَه: هَل أنتَ سَوَّيت وَسْطَهَا ... مُنيرًا إِذَا مَا جَنَّك الليَّل هاديا وقُولا لَهُ: مَنْ يُرْسِلُ الشَّمس غُدوةً ... فيُصبحَ مَا مَسَّتْ مِنَ الأرضِ ضَاحيا؟ ...

وَقُولا لَهُ: مَن يُنْبِت الحَبَّ فِي الثَّرَى ... فيُصبحَ مِنْه العُشب يَهَْتُّز رَابيا؟ ...

وَيُْخِرجُ منْه حَبَّه فِي رُءُوسِهِ ... فَفِي ذَاكَ آياتٌ لِمنْ كَانَ وَاعيَا 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ اسْتَوَى عَلَى الْعَرْشِ﴾ تَقَدَّمَ تَفْسِيرُ ذَلِكَ فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَعْرَافِ" وَأَنَّهُ يُمَرَّر كَمَا جَاءَ مِنْ غَيْرِ تَكْيِيفٍ، وَلَا تَشْبِيهٍ، وَلَا تَعْطِيلٍ، وَلَا تَمْثِيلٍ، تَعَالَى اللَّهُ عُلُوًّا كَبِيرًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَسَخَّرَ الشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ كُلٌّ يَجْرِي لأجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ أَنَّهُمَا يَجْرِيَانِ إِلَى انْقِطَاعِهِمَا بِقِيَامِ السَّاعَةِ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالشَّمْسُ تَجْرِي لِمُسْتَقَرٍّ لَهَا ذَلِكَ تَقْدِيرُ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ﴾ [يس: ٣٨] .

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ إِلَى مُسْتَقَرِّهِمَا، وَهُوَ تَحْتَ الْعَرْشِ مِمَّا يَلِي بَطْنَ الْأَرْضِ مِنَ الْجَانِبِ الْآخَرِ، فَإِنَّهُمَا وَسَائِرُ الْكَوَاكِبِ إِذَا وَصَلُوا هُنَالِكَ، يَكُونُونَ أَبْعَدَ مَا يَكُونُ عَنِ الْعَرْشِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ عَلَى الصَّحِيحِ الَّذِي تقومُ عَلَيْهِ الْأَدِلَّةُ، قُبَّةٌ مِمَّا يَلِي الْعَالَمِ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ، وَلَيْسَ بِمُحِيطٍ كَسَائِرِ الْأَفْلَاكِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ لَهُ قَوَائِمُ وَحَمَلَةٌ يَحْمِلُونَهُ. وَلَا يُتَصَوَّرُ هَذَا فِي الْفَلَكِ الْمُسْتَدِيرِ، وَهَذَا وَاضِحٌ لِمَنْ تَدَبَّر مَا وَرَدَتْ بِهِ الْآيَاتُ وَالْأَحَادِيثُ الصَّحِيحَةُ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ.

وَذَكَرَ الشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ؛ لِأَنَّهُمَا أَظْهَرُ الْكَوَاكِبِ السَّيَّارَةِ السَّبْعَةِ، الَّتِي هِيَ أَشْرَفُ وَأَعْظَمُ.

مِنَ الثَّوَابِتِ، فَإِذَا كَانَ قَدْ سَخَّرَ هَذِهِ، فَلأن يُدْخُلُ فِي التَّسْخِيرِ سائرُ الْكَوَاكِبِ بِطَرِيقِ الْأَوْلَى وَالْأَحْرَى، كَمَا نَبَّهَ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا تَسْجُدُوا لِلشَّمْسِ وَلا لِلْقَمَرِ وَاسْجُدُوا لِلَّهِ الَّذِي خَلَقَهُنَّ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ إِيَّاهُ تَعْبُدُونَ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٣٧] مَعَ أَنَّهُ قَدْ صَرَّحَ بِذَلِكَ بِقَوْلِهِ ﴿وَالشَّمْسَ وَالْقَمَرَ وَالنُّجُومَ مُسَخَّرَاتٍ بِأَمْرِهِ أَلا لَهُ الْخَلْقُ وَالأمْرُ تَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ رَبُّ الْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٥٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُفَصِّلُ الآيَاتِ لَعَلَّكُمْ بِلِقَاءِ رَبِّكُمْ تُوقِنُونَ﴾ أَيْ: يُوَضِّحُ الْآيَاتِ وَالدَّلَالَاتِ الدَّالَّةَ عَلَى أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَأَنَّهُ يُعِيدُ الْخَلْقَ إِذَا شَاءَ كَمَا ابْتَدَأَ خَلْقَهُ.

---

## 13:3-4 — verses 3-4 (shared commentary)

### Translation

After mentioning the higher realm, He, exalted is He, proceeded to mention His power, His wisdom, and His masterful arrangement of the lower realm, saying: {And He is the One who spread out the earth}, meaning: He made it wide, extended in length and breadth, and He anchored it with towering, firmly-set mountains, and He made rivers, streams, and springs flow within it to water the various fruits He placed in it, differing in colors, shapes, tastes, and scents, {of every kind, two mates}, meaning: of every form, two types.

{He causes the night to cover the day}, meaning: He made each of them pursue the other in swift pursuit, so when one departs, the other covers it, and when one ends, the other comes, thus He exercises His disposal over time just as He exercises His disposal over place and its inhabitants.

{Indeed in that are signs for a people who reflect}, meaning: upon the blessings of Allah, His wisdom, and His proofs.

His saying: {And in the earth are neighboring tracts}, meaning: lands that lie adjacent to one another, yet this one is good, producing what benefits people, while that one is salty and barren, producing nothing. This is what has been reported from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Dahhak, and others.

Likewise, included in this verse is the variation in the colors of the earth's regions: this soil is red, that one white, this one yellow, that one black, this one rocky and that one smooth, this one sandy, this one thick, this one thin, and all of them lie adjacent to one another. This one has its characteristic, and that one has its other characteristic. All of this points to the Doer who acts by free choice, there is no god but He, and no lord besides Him.

His saying: {and gardens of grapevines, and crops, and date palms}. It is possible that "crops" and "date palms" are conjoined to "gardens," in which case they would be in the nominative case. It is also possible that they are conjoined to "grapevines," in which case they would be in the genitive case. For this reason, a group of the leading scholars of recitation read it each of these two ways.

His saying: {sinwan (clustered from a single root) and non-sinwan}: al-sinwan refers to trunks that grow together from a single root, like the pomegranate, the fig, and some date palms, and similar things. Non-sinwan is what grows on a single, separate root, like most other trees. From this, a man's paternal uncle is called the sinw (counterpart) of his father, as has come in the sound hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Umar: "Did you not know that a man's paternal uncle is the sinw of his father?"

Sufyan al-Thawri and Shu'bah said, on the authority of Abu Ishaq, from al-Bara', may Allah be pleased with him: al-sinwan are the palm trees growing from a single root, and non-sinwan are the scattered ones. This was also said by Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam.

His saying: {watered with the same water, yet We favor some of them over others in food}. Al-A'mash reported, from Abu Salih, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding {yet We favor some of them over others in food}, that he said: "The inferior date and the superior date, the sweet and the sour." Reported by al-Tirmidhi, who said: hasan gharib (good, singular).

That is: this variation in the kinds of fruits and crops, in their shapes, colors, tastes, scents, leaves, and blossoms.

So this one is at the peak of sweetness and that one at the peak of sourness, this one at the peak of bitterness and that one is astringent, this one is mild and this one combines this and that, then it transforms into another taste by the permission of Allah, exalted is He. This one is yellow and that one is red, this one is white, that one is black, and this one is blue. Likewise the blossoms, even though all of them draw from a single source, namely water, yet with this great variation that cannot be confined or fully accounted for. In that are signs for whoever is heedful, and this is among the greatest proofs of the Doer who acts by free choice, who by His power made things differ from one another and created them as He willed. For this reason, He, exalted is He, said: {Indeed in that are signs for a people who reason}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى الْعَالَمَ الْعُلْوِيَّ، شَرَعَ فِي ذِكْرِ قُدْرَتِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ وَإِحْكَامِهِ لِلْعَالَمِ السُّفْلِيِّ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي مَدَّ الأرْضَ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلَهَا مُتَّسِعَةً مُمْتَدَّةً فِي الطُّولِ وَالْعَرْضِ، وَأَرْسَاهَا بِجِبَالٍ رَاسِيَاتٍ شَامِخَاتٍ، وَأَجْرَى فِيهَا الْأَنْهَارَ وَالْجَدَاوِلَ وَالْعُيُونَ لِسَقْيِ مَا جَعَلَ فِيهَا مِنَ الثَّمَرَاتِ الْمُخْتَلِفَةِ الْأَلْوَانِ وَالْأَشْكَالِ وَالطَّعُومِ وَالرَّوَائِحِ، مِنْ كُلِّ زَوْجَيْنِ اثْنَيْنِ، أَيْ: مِنْ كُلِّ شَكْلٍ صِنْفَانِ.

﴿يُغْشِي اللَّيْلَ النَّهَارَ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلَ كُلًّا مِنْهُمَا يَطْلُبُ الْآخَرَ طَلَبًا حَثِيثًا، فَإِذَا ذَهَبَ هَذَا غَشيه هَذَا، وَإِذَا انْقَضَى هَذَا جَاءَ الْآخَرُ، فَيَتَصَرَّفُ أَيْضًا فِي الزَّمَانِ كَمَا تَصَرَّفَ فِي الْمَكَانِ وَالسُّكَّانِ.

﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يَتَفَكَّرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي آلَاءِ اللَّهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ وَدَلَائِلِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَفِي الأرْضِ قِطَعٌ مُتَجَاوِرَاتٌ﴾ أَيْ: أراضٍ تُجَاوِرُ بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا، مَعَ أَنَّ هَذِهِ طَيِّبَةٌ تُنْبِتُ مَا يَنْتَفِعُ بِهِ النَّاسُ، وَهَذِهِ سَبَخة مَالِحَةٌ لَا تُنْبِتُ شَيْئًا. هَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَغَيْرِهِمْ.

وَكَذَا يَدْخُلُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ اخْتِلَافُ أَلْوَانِ بِقَاعِ الْأَرْضِ، فَهَذِهِ تُرْبَةٌ حَمْرَاءُ، وَهَذِهِ بَيْضَاءُ، وَهَذِهِ صَفْرَاءُ، وَهَذِهِ سَوْدَاءُ، وَهَذِهِ مُحَجَّرَةٌ وَهَذِهِ سَهْلَةٌ، وَهَذِهِ مُرَمَّلَةٌ، وَهَذِهِ سَمِيكَةٌ، وَهَذِهِ رَقِيقَةٌ، وَالْكُلُّ مُتَجَاوِرَاتٌ. فَهَذِهِ بِصِفَتِهَا، وَهَذِهِ بِصِفَتِهَا الْأُخْرَى، فَهَذَا كُلُّهُ مِمَّا يَدُلُّ عَلَى الْفَاعِلِ الْمُخْتَارِ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَجَنَّاتٌ مِنْ أَعْنَابٍ وَزَرْعٌ وَنَخِيلٌ﴾ يُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ عَاطِفَةً عَلَى ﴿جَنَّاتٍ﴾ فَيَكُونُ ﴿وَزَرْعٌ وَنَخِيلٌ﴾ مَرْفُوعَيْنِ. وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ يَكُونَ مَعْطُوفًا عَلَى أَعْنَابٍ، فَيَكُونُ مَجْرُورًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَرَأَ بِكُلٍّ مِنْهُمَا طَائِفَةٌ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿صِنْوَانٌ وَغَيْرُ صِنْوَانٍ﴾ الصِّنْوَانُ: هِيَ الْأُصُولُ الْمُجْتَمِعَةُ فِي مَنْبَتٍ وَاحِدٍ، كَالرُّمَّانِ وَالتِّينِ وَبَعْضِ النَّخِيلِ، وَنَحْوِ ذَلِكَ. وَغَيْرُ الصِّنْوَانِ: مَا كَانَ عَلَى أَصْلٍ وَاحِدٍ، كَسَائِرِ الْأَشْجَارِ، وَمِنْهُ سُمِّي عَمُّ الرَّجُلِ صِنْوُ أَبِيهِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ لِعُمَرَ: "أَمَّا شَعَرْتَ أَنَّ عَمَّ الرَّجُلِ صِنْوُ أَبِيهِ؟ " .

وَقَالَ سفيان الثوري، وشعبة، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الْبَرَاءِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: الصِّنْوَانُ: هِيَ النَّخْلَاتُ فِي أَصْلٍ وَاحِدٍ، وَغَيْرُ الصِّنْوَانِ: الْمُتَفَرِّقَاتُ. وَقَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُسْقَى بِمَاءٍ وَاحِدٍ وَنُفَضِّلُ بَعْضَهَا عَلَى بَعْضٍ فِي الأكُلِ﴾ قَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: ﴿وَنُفَضِّلُ بَعْضَهَا عَلَى بَعْضٍ فِي الأكُلِ﴾ قَالَ: "الدَّقَل وَالْفَارِسِيُّ، والحُلْو وَالْحَامِضُ". رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ .

أَيْ: هَذَا الِاخْتِلَافُ فِي أَجْنَاسِ الثَّمَرَاتِ وَالزُّرُوعِ، فِي أَشْكَالِهَا وَأَلْوَانِهَا، وَطَعُومِهَا وَرَوَائِحِهَا، وَأَوْرَاقِهَا وَأَزْهَارِهَا.

فَهَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْحَلَاوَةِ وَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْحُمُوضَةِ، وَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْمَرَارَةِ وَذَا عَفِص، وَهَذَا عَذْبٌ وَهَذَا جَمَعَ هَذَا وَهَذَا، ثُمَّ يَسْتَحِيلُ إِلَى طَعْمٍ آخَرَ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى. وَهَذَا أَصْفَرُ وَهَذَا أَحْمَرُ، وَهَذَا أَبْيَضُ وَهَذَا أَسْوَدُ وَهَذَا أَزْرَقُ. وَكَذَلِكَ الزُّهُورَاتُ مَعَ أَنَّ كُلَّهَا يُسْتَمَدُّ مِنْ طَبِيعَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ، وَهُوَ الْمَاءُ، مَعَ هَذَا الِاخْتِلَافِ الْكَبِيرِ الَّذِي لَا يَنْحَصِرُ وَلَا يَنْضَبِطُ، فَفِي ذَلِكَ آيَاتٌ لِمَنْ كَانَ وَاعِيًا، وَهَذَا مِنْ أَعْظَمِ الدَّلَالَاتِ عَلَى الْفَاعِلِ الْمُخْتَارِ، الَّذِي بِقُدْرَتِهِ فَاوَتَ بَيْنَ الْأَشْيَاءِ وَخَلَقَهَا عَلَى مَا يُرِيدُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِقَوْمٍ يَعْقِلُونَ﴾

---

## 13:5 — verse 5

### Translation

The Almighty says to His Messenger Muhammad ﷺ: {And if you are amazed}, at these polytheists' denial of the matter of the return, despite what they witness of the signs of Allah, glory be to Him, and His proofs in His creation showing that He is capable of whatever He wills, and despite their acknowledgment that He originated the creation of all things, bringing them into being after they had not been a thing mentioned at all. Yet after this they deny His report that He will bring the worlds back into being as a new creation, when they have already acknowledged and witnessed something more amazing than that which they deny. So the amazement is at their saying: {When we are dust, shall we indeed be in a new creation?} even though every knowledgeable and rational person knows that the creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind, and that whoever originated the creation, the repetition of it is easy for Him, as the Almighty said: {Have they not seen that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and was not wearied by their creation, is able to give life to the dead? Yes indeed, He has power over all things}

Then He described those who deny this, saying: {Those are the ones who have disbelieved in their Lord, and those will have shackles upon their necks}, meaning they will be dragged by them into the Fire, {and those are the companions of the Fire, they will abide therein forever}, meaning they will remain in it for all eternity, never removed from it and never departing from it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ: ﴿وَإِنْ تَعْجَبْ﴾ مِنْ تَكْذِيبِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ بِأَمْرِ الْمَعَادِ مَعَ مَا يُشَاهِدُونَهُ مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ سُبْحَانَهُ وَدَلَالَاتِهِ فِي خَلْقِهِ عَلَى أَنَّهُ الْقَادِرُ عَلَى مَا يَشَاءُ، وَمَعَ مَا يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِهِ مِنْ أَنَّهُ ابْتَدَأَ خَلْقَ الْأَشْيَاءِ، فَكَوَّنَهَا بَعْدَ أَنْ لَمْ تَكُنْ شَيْئًا مَذْكُورًا، ثُمَّ هُمْ بَعْدَ هَذَا يُكَذِّبُونَ خَبَرَهُ فِي أَنَّهُ سَيُعِيدُ الْعَالَمِينَ خَلْقًا جَدِيدًا، وَقَدِ اعْتَرَفُوا وَشَاهَدُوا مَا هُوَ أَعْجَبُ مِمَّا كَذَّبُوا بِهِ، فَالْعَجَبُ مِنْ قَوْلِهِمْ: ﴿أَئِذَا كُنَّا تُرَابًا أَئِنَّا لَفِي خَلْقٍ جَدِيدٍ﴾ وَقَدْ عَلِمَ كل عالم وعاقل أن خلق السموات وَالْأَرْضِ أَكْبَرُ مَنْ خَلْقِ النَّاسِ، وَأَنَّ مَنْ بَدَأَ الْخَلْقَ فَالْإِعَادَةُ سَهْلَةٌ عَلَيْهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّ اللَّهَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضَ وَلَمْ يَعْيَ بِخَلْقِهِنَّ بِقَادِرٍ عَلَى أَنْ يُحْيِيَ الْمَوْتَى بَلَى إِنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾

ثُمَّ نَعَتَ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ بِهَذَا فَقَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِرَبِّهِمْ وَأُولَئِكَ الأغْلالُ فِي أَعْنَاقِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُسْحَبُونَ بِهَا فِي النَّارِ، ﴿وَأُولَئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثُونَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا، لَا يُحَوَّلُونَ عَنْهَا وَلَا يَزُولُونَ.

---

## 13:6 — verse 6

### Translation

The Almighty says: {And they ask you to hasten} that is, these deniers, {the evil before the good} that is, punishment, as He informed about them in His saying: {And they said, "O you upon whom the reminder has been sent down, indeed you are mad. Why do you not bring us the angels, if you are among the truthful?" We do not send down the angels except with truth, and then they would not be given respite} [al-Hijr: 6-8]. And the Almighty said: {And they ask you to hasten the punishment. Were it not for a specified term, the punishment would have come to them, and it will surely come to them suddenly while they perceive not. They ask you to hasten the punishment, and indeed Hell surely encompasses the disbelievers} [al-Ankabut: 53, 54]. And He said: {A questioner asked about a punishment bound to happen} [al-Ma'arij: 1]. And He said: {Those who do not believe in it seek to hasten it, while those who believe are apprehensive of it and know that it is the truth} [al-Shura: 18]. {And they said, "Our Lord, hasten for us our share before the Day of Reckoning"} [Sad: 16], that is, our reckoning and our punishment, as He said, informing about them: {And when they said, "O Allah, if this is indeed the truth from You, then rain down upon us stones from the sky or bring us a painful punishment"} [al-Anfal: 32]. So they used to demand of the Messenger that he bring them the punishment of Allah, and that was due to the intensity of their denial, their disbelief, and their obstinacy.

Allah the Almighty says: {And there have already passed before them similar exemplary punishments} that is, We had already inflicted Our vengeance upon the past nations and made them an example, a lesson, and an admonition for whoever takes heed from them.

Then the Almighty informs that were it not for His forbearance, His pardon, and His forgiveness, He would have dealt with them by punishment, as the Almighty said: {And if Allah were to seize mankind for what they have earned, He would not leave upon its back any creature} [Fatir: 45].

And the Almighty said in this noble verse: {And indeed your Lord is full of forgiveness for people despite their wrongdoing} that is, He possesses pardon, forbearance, and concealment for people despite the fact that they commit wrong and err by night and day. Then He coupled this ruling with the fact that He is severe in punishment, so that hope and fear might be balanced, as the Almighty said: {But if they deny you, then say, "Your Lord is possessed of vast mercy, but His might cannot be averted from the wrongdoing people"} [al-An'am: 147]. And He said: {Indeed your Lord is swift in punishment, and indeed He is Forgiving, Merciful} [al-A'raf: 167]. And He said: {Inform My servants that I am indeed the Forgiving, the Merciful, and that My punishment is indeed the painful punishment} [al-Hijr: 49, 50], and other similar verses that combine hope and fear.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Musa ibn Isma'il narrated to us, Hammad narrated to us, from Ali ibn Zayd, from Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, who said: When this verse was revealed, {And indeed your Lord is full of forgiveness for people despite their wrongdoing, and indeed your Lord is severe in punishment}, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Were it not for Allah's pardon and His overlooking, no one would find life pleasant, and were it not for His warning and His punishment, everyone would rely entirely on that pardon."

The Hafiz Ibn Asakir narrated, in the biographical entry on al-Hasan ibn Uthman Abu Hassan al-Ziyadi, that he saw the Lord of Might in a dream, with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ standing before Him interceding for a man of his ummah. He said to him: "Was it not enough for you that I sent down to you in Surat al-Ra'd: {And indeed your Lord is full of forgiveness for people despite their wrongdoing}?" He said: then I awoke.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ﴾ أَيْ: هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ ﴿بِالسَّيِّئَةِ قَبْلَ الْحَسَنَةِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْعُقُوبَةِ، كَمَا أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَقَالُوا يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِي نزلَ عَلَيْهِ الذِّكْرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجْنُونٌ * لَوْ مَا تَأْتِينَا بِالْمَلائِكَةِ إِنْ كُنْتَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ * مَا نُنزلُ الْمَلائِكَةَ إِلا بِالْحَقِّ وَمَا كَانُوا إِذًا مُنْظَرِينَ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:٦ -٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَلَوْلا أَجَلٌ مُسَمًّى لَجَاءَهُمُ الْعَذَابُ وَلَيَأْتِيَنَّهُمْ بَغْتَةً وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ * يَسْتَعْجِلُونَكَ بِالْعَذَابِ وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمُحِيطَةٌ بِالْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ: ٥٣، ٥٤] وَقَالَ: ﴿سَأَلَ سَائِلٌ بِعَذَابٍ وَاقِعٍ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ: ١] وَقَالَ: ﴿يَسْتَعْجِلُ بِهَا الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهَا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مُشْفِقُونَ مِنْهَا وَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهَا الْحَقُّ﴾ [الشُّورَى: ١٨] ﴿وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا عَجِّلْ لَنَا قِطَّنَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ [ص: ١٦] أَيْ: حِسَابَنَا وَعِقَابَنَا، كَمَا قَالَ مُخْبِرًا عَنْهُمْ: ﴿وَإِذْ قَالُوا اللَّهُمَّ إِنْ كَانَ هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقَّ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ فَأَمْطِرْ عَلَيْنَا حِجَارَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ أَوِ ائْتِنَا بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ: ٣٢] فَكَانُوا يَطْلُبُونَ مِنَ الرَّسُولِ أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُمْ بِعَذَابِ اللَّهِ، وَذَلِكَ مِنْ شِدَّةِ تَكْذِيبِهِمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقَدْ خَلَتْ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمُ الْمَثُلاتُ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أَوْقَعْنَا نِقْمَتَنَا بِالْأُمَمِ الْخَالِيَةِ وَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ مُثْلَةً وَعِبْرَةً وَعِظَةً لِمَنِ اتَّعَظَ بِهِمْ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَوْلَا حلمه وعفوه [وغفره] لعالجهم بِالْعُقُوبَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ يُؤَاخِذُ اللَّهُ النَّاسَ بِمَا كَسَبُوا مَا تَرَكَ عَلَى ظَهْرِهَا مِنْ دَابَّةٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ٤٥] .

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَذُو مَغْفِرَةٍ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَى ظُلْمِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّهُ ذُو عَفْوٍ وَصَفْحٍ وَسَتْرٍ لِلنَّاسِ مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ وَيُخْطِئُونَ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ. ثُمَّ قَرَنَ هَذَا الْحُكْمَ بِأَنَّهُ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ، لِيَعْتَدِلَ الرَّجَاءُ وَالْخَوْفُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَإِنْ كَذَّبُوكَ فَقُلْ رَبُّكُمْ ذُو رَحْمَةٍ وَاسِعَةٍ وَلا يُرَدُّ بَأْسُهُ عَنِ الْقَوْمِ الْمُجْرِمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٤٧] وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَسَرِيعُ الْعِقَابِ وَإِنَّهُ لَغَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٦٧] وَقَالَ: ﴿نَبِّئْ عِبَادِي أَنِّي أَنَا الْغَفُورُ الرَّحِيمُ وَأَنَّ عَذَابِي هُوَ الْعَذَابُ الألِيمُ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ:٤٩، ٥٠] إِلَى أَمْثَالِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الَّتِي تَجْمَعُ الرَّجَاءَ وَالْخَوْفَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ المسَيَّب قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَذُو مَغْفِرَةٍ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَى ظُلْمِهِمْ وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَشَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَوْلَا عفوُ اللَّهِ وتجاوُزه، مَا هَنَّأَ أَحَدًا الْعَيْشَ وَلَوْلَا وَعِيدُهُ وَعِقَابُهُ، لَاتَّكَلَ كُلُّ أَحَدٍ" .

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عُثْمَانَ أَبِي حَسَّانَ الزِّيَادَيِّ: أَنَّهُ رَأَى رَبَّ الْعِزَّةِ فِي النَّوْمِ، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَاقِفٌ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ يُشَفَّعُ فِي رَجُلٍ مِنْ أُمَّتِهِ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: أَلَمْ يَكْفِكَ أَنِّي أَنْزَلْتُ عَلَيْكَ فِي سُورَةِ الرَّعْدِ: ﴿وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَذُو مَغْفِرَةٍ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَى ظُلْمِهِمْ﴾ ؟ قَالَ: ثُمَّ انْتَبَهْتُ.

---

## 13:7 — verse 7

### Translation

The Exalted says, informing about the polytheists, that they say out of disbelief and stubbornness: why does he not bring us a sign from his Lord as the earlier ones were sent, just as they demanded of him that he turn al-Safa into gold for them, and that he remove the mountains from them and put in their place meadows and rivers. God the Exalted said: {And nothing has prevented Us from sending signs except that the earlier peoples denied them. And We gave Thamud the she-camel as a visible sign, but they wronged her. And We do not send signs except as a warning} [al-Isra: 59].

God the Exalted said: {You are only a warner}, meaning: your only duty is to convey the message of God which He has commanded you to deliver, {Their guidance is not your responsibility, but God guides whom He wills} [al-Baqarah: 272].

Concerning His saying, {And for every people there is a guide}, Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, that it means: for every people there is a caller.

Al-Awfi said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, in explaining the two verses together: God the Exalted says: you, O Muhammad, are a warner, and I am the guide of every people. Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Dahhak said likewise.

From Mujahid: {And for every people there is a guide}, meaning: a prophet. As He said: {And there was no nation but a warner had passed among them} [Fatir: 24]. Qatadah and Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd said the same.

Abu Salih and Yahya ibn Rafi' said: {And for every people there is a guide} means: a leader.

Abu al-Aliyah said: the guide is the leader, and the leader is the imam, and the imam is the deed (al-'amal).

From Ikrimah and Abu al-Duha: {And for every people there is a guide}, they both said it refers to Muhammad, the Messenger of God ﷺ.

Malik said: {And for every people there is a guide} means whoever calls them to God, Mighty and Majestic is He.

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: Ahmad ibn Yahya al-Sufi narrated to me, al-Hasan ibn al-Husayn al-Ansari narrated to us, Mu'adh ibn Muslim, the cloth-seller of Herat, narrated to us, from Ata' ibn al-Sa'ib, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with them both, who said: when {You are only a warner, and for every people there is a guide} was revealed, the Messenger of God ﷺ placed his hand upon his chest and said, "I am the warner, and for every people there is a guide," and he gestured with his hand toward the shoulder of Ali and said, "You are the guide, O Ali. Through you those who are rightly guided after me will be guided."

This hadith contains severe munkar (objectionable/unrecognized narration).

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ali ibn al-Husayn narrated to us, Uthman ibn Abi Shaybah narrated to us, al-Muttalib ibn Ziyad narrated to us, from al-Suddi, from Abd Khayr, from Ali: {And for every people there is a guide}, he said: the guide is a man from Banu Hashim. Al-Junayd said: he is Ali ibn Abi Talib, may God be pleased with him.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: something similar has been reported from Ibn Abbas in one of the narrations, and from Abu Ja'far Muhammad ibn Ali.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنِ الْمُشْرِكِينَ أَنَّهُمْ يَقُولُونَ كُفْرًا وَعِنَادًا: لَوْلَا يَأْتِينَا بِآيَةٍ مِنْ ربه كما أرسل الأولون، كما تعتنوا عَلَيْهِ أَنْ يَجْعَلَ لَهُمُ الصَّفَا ذَهَبَا، وَأَنْ يُزِيلَ عَنْهُمُ الْجِبَالَ، وَيَجْعَلَ مَكَانَهَا مُرُوجًا وَأَنْهَارًا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا مَنَعَنَا أَنْ نُرْسِلَ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا أَنْ كَذَّبَ بِهَا الأوَّلُونَ وَآتَيْنَا ثَمُودَ النَّاقَةَ مُبْصِرَةً فَظَلَمُوا بِهَا وَمَا نُرْسِلُ بِالآيَاتِ إِلا تَخْوِيفًا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٥٩] .

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ مُنْذِرٌ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا عَلَيْكَ أَنْ تُبَلِّغَ رِسَالَةَ اللَّهِ الَّتِي أَمَرَكَ بِهَا، ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَيْكَ هُدَاهُمْ وَلَكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٧٢] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، أَيْ: وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ دَاعٍ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِمَا: يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: أَنْتَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ مُنْذِرٌ، وَأَنَا هَادِي كُلَّ قَوْمٍ، وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ.

وَعَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ أَيْ: نَبِيٌّ. كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ مِنْ أُمَّةٍ إِلا خَلا فِيهَا نَذِيرٌ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ٢٤] وَبِهِ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو صَالِحٍ، وَيَحْيَى بْنُ رَافِعٍ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ أَيْ: قَائِدٍ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: الْهَادِي: الْقَائِدُ، وَالْقَائِدُ: الْإِمَامُ، وَالْإِمَامُ: الْعَمَلُ.

وَعَنْ عِكْرِمة، وَأَبِي الضُّحَى: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ قَالَا هُوَ مُحَمَّدٍ [رَسُولِ اللَّهِ] ﷺ.

وَقَالَ مَالِكٌ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ مَنْ يَدْعُوهُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي أَحْمَدُ بْنُ يَحْيَى الصُّوفِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعَاذُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ بَيَّاعٌ الْهَرَوِيِّ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ مُنْذِرٌ وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ قَالَ: وَضَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَدَهُ عَلَى صَدْرِهِ، وَقَالَ: "أَنَا الْمُنْذِرُ، وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ". وَأَوْمَأَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى مَنْكِبِ عَلَيٍّ، فَقَالَ: "أَنْتَ الْهَادِي يَا عَلِيُّ، بِكَ يَهْتَدِي الْمُهْتَدُونَ مِنْ بَعْدِي".

وهذا الحديث فيه نكارة شديدة .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُطَّلِبُ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، عَنِ السُّدِّيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ خَيْرٍ، عَنْ عَلَيٍّ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ﴾ قَالَ: الْهَادِي: رَجُلٌ مِنْ بَنِي هَاشِمٍ: قَالَ الْجُنَيْدُ هُوَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: وَرُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، فِي إِحْدَى الرِّوَايَاتِ، وَعَنْ أَبِي جَعْفَرٍ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، نَحْوَ ذَلِكَ.

---

## 13:8-9 — verses 8-9 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us of the completeness of His knowledge, from which nothing is hidden, and that He encompasses what every pregnant female of every kind of creature carries, as the Almighty said: {And He knows what is in the wombs} [Luqman: 34], meaning: what she carries, whether male or female, comely or unsightly, wretched or blessed, long-lived or short-lived, as the Almighty said: {He is most knowing of you when He produced you from the earth and when you were embryos in the wombs of your mothers. So do not claim yourselves to be pure; He is most knowing of who fears Him} [al-Najm: 32].

And the Almighty said: {He creates you in the wombs of your mothers, creation after creation, within three darknesses} [al-Zumar: 6], meaning: He created you stage after stage, as the Almighty said: {And certainly did We create man from an extract of clay. Then We placed him as a sperm-drop in a firm lodging. Then We made the sperm-drop into a clinging clot, and We made the clot into a lump of flesh, and We made the lump into bones, and We covered the bones with flesh; then We developed him into another creation. So blessed is Allah, the best of creators} [al-Mu'minun: 12-14]. In the two Sahihs, from Ibn Mas'ud, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed the creation of one of you is gathered in his mother's womb for forty days, then he is a clinging clot for a similar period, then he is a lump of flesh for a similar period, then an angel is sent to him and is commanded with four matters: he writes down his provision, his lifespan, his deeds, and whether he is wretched or blessed."

And in another hadith: "Then the angel says: O Lord, is it male or female? O Lord, is it wretched or blessed? What is its provision? What is its appointed term? So Allah says, and the angel writes."

Concerning His saying, {And whatever the wombs diminish or exceed}, al-Bukhari said: [chain] ... Ibn 'Umar, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The keys of the unseen are five, which none knows but Allah: none knows what is in tomorrow except Allah, none knows what the wombs diminish except Allah, none knows when the rain will come except Allah, no soul knows in what land it will die, and none knows when the Hour will come except Allah."

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: {And whatever the wombs diminish} means: the miscarried fetus, {or exceed} means: what the womb adds to the pregnancy beyond what it diminished, until it gives birth to it complete. This is because among women there are those who carry for ten months, and those who carry for nine months, and those whose pregnancy is prolonged, and those whose pregnancy is shortened. That is the diminishing and increasing which Allah the Almighty mentioned, and all of that is by His knowledge, the Almighty.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn 'Abbas, concerning His saying: {And whatever the wombs diminish or exceed}, he said: what is less than nine months and what is more than it.

Al-Dahhak said: My mother gave birth to me after having carried me in her womb for two years, and she bore me with my front tooth already grown.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Jamilah bint Sa'd, from 'A'ishah, who said: Pregnancy does not exceed two years, the span in which the shadow of a spindle would move.

Mujahid said: {And whatever the wombs diminish or exceed}, he said: what she sees of blood during her pregnancy, and what exceeds nine months. 'Atiyyah al-'Awfi, Qatadah, al-Hasan al-Basri, and al-Dahhak said the same.

Mujahid also said: If a woman sees blood during less than nine months, it is added onto the nine months, the equivalent of the days of menstruation. 'Ikrimah, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and Ibn Zayd said likewise.

Mujahid also said: {And whatever the wombs diminish} is the woman's discharge of blood, causing the child to become deficient, {or exceed}, if the woman does not discharge blood, the child becomes complete and grows large.

Makhul said: The fetus in its mother's womb does not seek, does not grieve, and does not sorrow. Rather, its provision comes to it in its mother's womb from her menstrual blood, and that is why a pregnant woman does not menstruate. When it falls to the earth, it cries out, and its crying out is a protest at its new situation. When its umbilical cord is cut, Allah transfers its provision to its mother's two breasts, so that it does not seek, does not grieve, and does not sorrow. Then it becomes a small child who takes hold of a thing with its hand and eats it. Then when it reaches maturity, it says: "It is death, or it is being killed. From where will I get provision?" Makhul then says: "Woe to you! He nourished you when you were in your mother's womb, and when you were a small child, until when you grew strong and gained reason, you said: 'It is death, or it is being killed. From where will I get provision?'" Then Makhul recited: {Allah knows what every female carries and what the wombs diminish or exceed, and everything with Him is by due measure}.

Qatadah said: {and everything with Him is by due measure}, meaning: by an appointed term. He has preserved the provisions of His creation and their appointed terms, and He has set for that a known term.

In the sound hadith: one of the daughters of the Prophet ﷺ sent to him saying that a son of hers was dying, and that she wished for him to be present. So he sent to her, saying: "To Allah belongs what He has taken, and to Him belongs what He has given, and everything with Him is for an appointed term. So command her to be patient and to seek reward," the hadith in full.

Concerning His saying, {Knower of the unseen and the witnessed}, meaning: He knows everything, both what His servants witness and what is hidden from them, and nothing of it is hidden from Him. {The Grand}, who is greater than everything, {the Most High}, meaning: above everything. He has encompassed everything in knowledge, and has overpowered everything, so that necks have bowed to Him and His servants have submitted to Him, willingly or unwillingly.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَمَامِ عِلْمِهِ الَّذِي لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ، وَأَنَّهُ مُحِيطٌ بِمَا تَحْمِلُهُ الْحَوَامِلُ مِنْ كُلِّ إِنَاثِ الْحَيَوَانَاتِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَعْلَمُ مَا فِي الأرْحَامِ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٣٤] أَيْ: مَا حَمَلَتْ مِنْ ذِكْرٍ أَوْ أُنْثَى، أَوْ حَسَنٍ أَوْ قَبِيحٍ، أَوْ شَقِيٍّ أَوْ سَعِيدٍ، أَوْ طَوِيلِ الْعُمُرِ أَوْ قَصِيرُهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِكُمْ إِذْ أَنْشَأَكُمْ مِنَ الأرْضِ وَإِذْ أَنْتُمْ أَجِنَّةٌ فِي بُطُونِ أُمَّهَاتِكُمْ فَلا تُزَكُّوا أَنْفُسَكُمْ هُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِمَنِ اتَّقَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣٢] .

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَخْلُقُكُمْ فِي بُطُونِ أُمَّهَاتِكُمْ خَلْقًا مِنْ بَعْدِ خَلْقٍ فِي ظُلُمَاتٍ ثَلاثٍ﴾ [الزُّمَرِ:٦] أَيْ: خَلَقَكُمْ طَوْرًا مِنْ بَعْدِ طَوْرٍ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا الإنْسَانَ مِنْ سُلالَةٍ مِنْ طِينٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلْنَاهُ نُطْفَةً فِي قَرَارٍ مَكِينٍ ثُمَّ خَلَقْنَا النُّطْفَةَ عَلَقَةً فَخَلَقْنَا الْعَلَقَةَ مُضْغَةً فَخَلَقْنَا الْمُضْغَةَ عِظَامًا فَكَسَوْنَا الْعِظَامَ لَحْمًا ثُمَّ أَنْشَأْنَاهُ خَلْقًا آخَرَ فَتَبَارَكَ اللَّهُ أَحْسَنُ الْخَالِقِينَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١٢: ١٤] وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم: "إِنَّ خَلْقَ أَحَدِكُمْ يُجْمَعُ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ عَلَقَةً مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ مضغة مثل ذلك، ثم يبعث إِلَيْهِ مَلَكٌ فَيُؤْمَرُ بِأَرْبَعِ كَلِمَاتٍ: يَكْتب رِزْقَهُ، وَعُمُرَهُ، وَعَمَلَهُ، وَشِقِّيٌ أَوْ سَعِيدٌ" .

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "فَيَقُولُ الْمَلَكُ: أيْ رَبِّ، أَذَكَرٌ أَمْ أُنْثَى؟ أَيْ رَبِّ، أَشَقِيٌّ أَمْ سَعِيدٌ؟ فَمَا الرِّزْقُ؟ فَمَا الْأَجَلُ؟ فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ، وَيَكْتُبُ الْمَلَكُ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ وَمَا تَزْدَادُ﴾ قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْن، حَدَّثَنَا مَالِكٌ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَفَاتِيحُ الْغَيْبِ خَمْسٌ لَا يَعْلَمُهَا إِلَّا اللَّهُ: لَا يَعْلَمُ مَا فِي غَدٍ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَا يَعْلَمُ مَا تَغِيضُ الْأَرْحَامُ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَا يَعْلَمُ مَتَى يَأْتِي الْمَطَرُ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَا تَدْرِي نَفْسٌ بِأَيِّ أَرْضٍ تَمُوتُ، وَلَا يَعْلَمُ مَتَى تقوم الساعة إلا الله" .

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ﴾ يَعْنِي: السَقْط ﴿وَمَا تَزْدَادُ﴾ يَقُولُ: مَا زَادَتِ الرَّحِمَ فِي الْحَمْلِ عَلَى مَا غَاضَتْ حَتَّى وَلَدَتْهُ تَمَامًا. وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ مَنْ تَحْمِلُ عَشْرَةَ أَشْهُرَ، وَمِنْهُنَّ مَنْ تَحْمِلُ تِسْعَةَ أَشْهُرَ، وَمِنْهُنَّ مَنْ تَزِيدُ فِي الْحَمْلِ، وَمِنْهُنَّ مَنْ تَنْقُصُ، فَذَلِكَ الْغَيْضُ وَالزِّيَادَةُ الَّتِي ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، وَكُلُّ ذَلِكَ بِعِلْمِهِ تَعَالَى.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ وَمَا تَزْدَادُ﴾ قَالَ: مَا نَقَصَتْ مِنْ تِسْعَةٍ وَمَا زَادَ عَلَيْهَا.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: وَضَعَتْنِي أُمِّي وَقَدْ حَمَلَتْنِي فِي بَطْنِهَا سَنَتَيْنِ، وَوَلَدَتْنِي وَقَدْ نَبَتَتْ ثنيَّتي.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنْ جَمِيلَةَ بِنْتِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: لَا يَكُونُ الْحَمْلُ أَكْثَرَ مِنْ سَنَتَيْنِ، قَدْرَ مَا يَتَحَرَّكُ ظِل مغْزَل.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ وَمَا تَزْدَادُ﴾ قَالَ: مَا تَرَى مِنَ الدَّمِ فِي حَمْلِهَا، وَمَا تَزْدَادُ عَلَى تِسْعَةِ أَشْهُرٍ. وَبِهِ قَالَ عَطِيَّةُ الْعَوْفِيُّ وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ أَيْضًا: إِذَا رَأَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ الدَّمَ دُونَ التِّسْعَةِ زَادَ عَلَى التِّسْعَةِ، مِثْلَ أَيَّامِ الْحَيْضِ. وَقَالَهُ عِكْرِمة، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ أَيْضًا: ﴿وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ﴾ إِرَاقَةُ الْمَرْأَةِ حَتَّى يَخِسَّ الْوَلَدُ ﴿وَمَا تَزْدَادُ﴾ إِنْ لَمْ تُهْرِقِ الْمَرْأَةُ تَمَّ الْوَلَدُ وَعَظُمَ.

وَقَالَ مَكْحُولٌ: الْجَنِينُ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ لَا يَطْلُبُ، وَلَا يَحْزَنُ وَلَا يَغْتَمُّ، وَإِنَّمَا يَأْتِيهِ رِزْقُهُ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ مِنْ دَمِ حَيْضَتِهَا فَمِنْ ثَمَّ لَا تَحِيضُ الْحَامِلُ. فَإِذَا وَقَعَ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ اسْتَهَلَّ، وَاسْتِهْلَالُهُ اسْتِنْكَارٌ لِمَكَانِهِ، فَإِذَا قُطِعَتْ سُرَّتُهُ حَوَّلَ اللَّهُ رِزْقَهُ إِلَى ثَدْيَيْ أُمِّهِ حَتَّى لَا يَطْلُبَ وَلَا يَحْزَنَ وَلَا يَغْتَمَّ، ثُمَّ يَصِيرُ طِفْلًا يَتَنَاوَلُ الشَّيْءَ بِكَفِّهِ فَيَأْكُلُهُ، فَإِذَا هُوَ بَلَغَ قَالَ: هُوَ الْمَوْتُ أَوِ الْقَتْلُ، أنَّى لِي بِالرِّزْقِ؟ فَيَقُولُ مَكْحُولٌ: يَا وَيْلَكَ ! غَذاك وَأَنْتَ فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّكَ، وَأَنْتَ طِفْلٌ صَغِيرٌ، حَتَّى إِذَا اشْتَدَدْتَ وَعَقَلْتَ قُلْتَ: هُوَ الْمَوْتُ أَوِ الْقَتْلُ، أَنَّى لِي بِالرِّزْقِ؟ ثُمَّ قَرَأَ مَكْحُولٌ: ﴿اللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مَا تَحْمِلُ كُلُّ أُنْثَى وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ وَمَا تَزْدَادُ وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ عِنْدَهُ بِمِقْدَارٍ﴾

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ عِنْدَهُ بِمِقْدَارٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِأَجْلٍ، حَفِظَ أَرْزَاقَ خَلْقِهِ وَآجَالَهُمْ، وَجَعَلَ لِذَلِكَ أَجَلًا مَعْلُومًا.

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ إِحْدَى بَنَاتِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بَعَثَتْ إِلَيْهِ: أَنَّ ابْنًا لَهَا فِي الْمَوْتِ، وَأَنَّهَا تُحِبُّ أَنْ يَحْضُرَهُ. فَبَعَثَ إِلَيْهَا يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَا أَخَذَ، وَلَهُ مَا أَعْطَى، وَكُلُّ شَيْءٍ عِنْدَهُ بِأَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى، فَمُرُوهَا فَلْتَصْبِرْ وَلِتَحْتَسِبْ" الْحَدِيثَ بِتَمَامِهِ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿عَالِمُ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْلَمُ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ مِمَّا يُشَاهِدُهُ الْعِبَادُ وَمِمَّا يَغِيبُ عَنْهُمْ، وَلَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ. ﴿الْكَبِيرُ﴾ الَّذِي هُوَ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، ﴿الْمُتَعَالِ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، قَدْ أَحَاطَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عِلْمًا، وَقَهَرَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، فَخَضَعَتْ لَهُ الرِّقَابُ وَدَانَ لَهُ الْعِبَادُ، طَوْعًا وَكَرْهًا.

---

## 13:10-11 — verses 10-11 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs of the encompassing of His knowledge over all His creation, whether they conceal their speech or utter it openly. He hears it, and nothing is hidden from Him, as He said: {And if you speak the word aloud, then indeed He knows the secret and what is even more hidden} [Ta-Ha: 7], and He said: {And He knows what you conceal and what you proclaim} [al-Naml: 25]. 'A'isha, may Allah be pleased with her, said: "Glory be to the One whose hearing encompasses all voices. By Allah, the woman who disputed came complaining about her husband to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ while I was at the side of the house, and some of her speech was hidden from me, so Allah revealed: {Allah has indeed heard the speech of the one who disputes with you concerning her husband and complains to Allah. And Allah hears your dialogue. Indeed Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing} [al-Mujadalah: 1]."

His statement: {and whoever is concealed in the night} means: hidden in the depths of his house in the darkness of night, {and one who moves about openly in the day} means: apparent, walking about in the brightness and light of day. Both of these are equal in Allah's knowledge, as the Exalted said: {Indeed, when they cover themselves with their garments, He knows what they conceal and what they proclaim} [Hud: 5], and the Exalted said: {And you are not [engaged] in any matter, and you do not recite any portion of the Qur'an, and you do not do any deed, except that We are witnesses over you when you are engaged in it. And nothing is hidden from your Lord, not even the weight of a speck of dust, in the earth or in the heaven, nor anything smaller than that or greater, except that it is in a clear record} [Yunus: 61].

His statement: {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him, who guard him by the command of Allah} means: for the servant there are angels who take turns over him, a guard by night and a guard by day, guarding him from misfortunes and calamities, just as other angels take turns to record deeds, whether good or bad, angels by night and angels by day. Two of them are on the right and on the left, writing down deeds; the one on the right writes down good deeds, and the one on the left writes down bad deeds. And two other angels guard and watch over him, one behind him and another before him. So he is between four angels by day and another four by night in rotation, two guardians and two recorders, as has come in the authentic hadith: "Angels take turns over you, angels by night and angels by day, and they gather at the dawn prayer and the afternoon prayer. Then those who spent the night among you ascend, and He asks them, though He is most knowing about you: 'How did you leave My servants?' They say: 'We came to them while they were praying, and we left them while they were praying.'" And in another hadith: "Indeed with you is one who does not part from you except at the time of relieving oneself and at the time of intercourse, so have modesty before them and honor them."

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, from Ibn Abbas: {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him, who guard him by the command of Allah}: the succeeding ones are by the command of Allah, and they are the angels.

Ikrima said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {who guard him by the command of Allah}: he said: angels guard him from before him and from behind him, but when the decree of Allah comes, they leave him.

Mujahid said: there is no servant except that he has an angel appointed to him, who guards him in his sleep and his waking from the jinn, mankind, and crawling creatures. Whenever any of these approaches wanting to harm him, the angel says: "Behind you!" except for something that Allah permits, which then befalls him.

Al-Thawri said, from Habib ibn Abi Thabit, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him}: he said: that refers to a king among the kings of the world, who has guards, and beneath him more guards.

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him}: it means: the ally of Satan, over whom there are guards. And Ikrima said in explaining it: these are the commanders, the processions before him and behind him.

Al-Dahhak said, regarding {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him, who guard him by the command of Allah}: he said: this is the ruler who is guarded from the decree of Allah, and they are the people of shirk (polytheism).

The apparent meaning, and Allah knows best, is that what Ibn Abbas, Ikrima, and al-Dahhak intended by this is that the guarding of the angels over the servants resembles the guarding that these guards provide for their kings and commanders.

The imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir has narrated here a very gharib (singular) hadith, saying:

[chain] Kinana al-'Adawi said: Uthman ibn Affan came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said: "O Messenger of Allah, tell me about the servant, how many angels are with him?" He said: "An angel on your right over your good deeds, who is in charge over the one on the left. When you do a good deed, it is recorded tenfold. When you do a bad deed, the one on the left says to the one on the right: 'Shall I write it?' He says: 'No, perhaps he will seek Allah's forgiveness and repent.' If he says it three times, he says: 'Yes, write it, Allah has relieved us of him, what an evil companion. How little he is mindful of Allah, and how little he is ashamed before us.'" Allah says: {He does not utter any word except that with him is an observer, ready [to record]} [Qaf: 18]. "And two angels are before you and behind you." Allah says: {He has succeeding angels, before him and behind him, who guard him by the command of Allah}. "And an angel grips your forelock; when you humble yourself before Allah, He raises you, and when you act arrogantly toward Allah, He breaks you. And two angels are on your lips, guarding nothing over you except the invoking of blessings upon Muhammad ﷺ. And an angel stands over your mouth, not letting a snake enter your mouth. And two angels are over your eyes. These are ten angels over every human being, and the angels of the night descend upon the angels of the day, for the angels of the night are other than the angels of the day. So these are twenty angels over every human being, along with Iblis by day and his offspring by night."

The imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Abdullah said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is not one of you except that his companion from the jinn has been appointed over him, and his companion from the angels." They said: "And you too, O Messenger of Allah?" He said: "And me too, but Allah has helped me against him, so he only commands me to do good."

Muslim alone has recorded this.

His statement: {who guard him by the command of Allah}: it is said that what is meant is their guarding of him from the command of Allah. This was narrated by Ali ibn Abi Talha and others from Ibn Abbas, and this is the view held by Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and others.

Qatada said, regarding {who guard him by the command of Allah}: he said: and in some recitations it reads: "who guard him by the command of Allah [bi-amri Allah]."

Ka'b al-Ahbar said: If every plain and rugged place were made manifest to the son of Adam, he would see everything of that as devils, were it not that Allah has appointed angels over you regarding your food, your drink, and your private parts. Otherwise, you would be snatched away.

Abu Umama said: There is no human being except that with him is an angel who wards off harm from him, until he hands him over to what has been decreed for him.

Abu Mijlaz said: A man from Murad came to Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, while he was praying, and said: "Be on guard, for people from Murad want to kill you." He said: "With every man are two angels who guard him from what has not been decreed. But when the decree comes, they leave him to it. And the appointed term is a fortified shield."

Some of them said: {who guard him by the command of Allah} means by the command of Allah, as has come in the hadith that they said: "O Messenger of Allah, what do you think of the incantations by which we seek healing, do they repel anything of Allah's decree?" He said: "They are part of Allah's decree."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibrahim said: Allah revealed to a prophet among the prophets of the Children of Israel: Say to your people: There is no people of a town, nor people of a household, who are in obedience to Allah and then turn from it to disobedience of Allah, except that what they love is turned for them into what they dislike. Then he said: The confirmation of this is in the Book of Allah: {Indeed, Allah does not change the condition of a people until they change what is in themselves}.

This has also come in a marfu' (elevated) hadith. Al-Hafiz Muhammad ibn Uthman ibn Abi Shayba said in his book "Sifat al-'Arsh": [chain] Umayr ibn Abdullah said: Ali ibn Abi Talib delivered a sermon to us on the pulpit of Kufa, and said: When I was silent regarding the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he would initiate speech with me, and when I asked him about a report, he would inform me. And he related to me from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, saying: "The Lord said: By My might and My majesty, and My elevation above My throne, there is no people of a town nor people of a household who were upon what I dislike of disobedience to Me, and then turned from it to what I love of obedience to Me, except that I turn for them from what they dislike of My punishment to what they love of My mercy."

This is gharib (singular), and in its chain of transmission there is someone I do not know.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ إِحَاطَةِ عِلْمِهِ بِجَمِيعِ خَلْقِهِ، سَوَاءٌ مِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَسَرَّ قَوْلَهُ أَوْ جَهَرَ بِهِ، فَإِنَّهُ يَسْمَعُهُ لَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ تَجْهَرْ بِالْقَوْلِ فَإِنَّهُ يَعْلَمُ السِّرَّ وَأَخْفَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٧] وَقَالَ: ﴿وَيَعْلَمُ مَا تُخْفُونَ وَمَا تُعْلِنُونَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ٢٥] وَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي وَسِعَ سَمْعُهُ الْأَصْوَاتَ، وَاللَّهِ لَقَدْ جَاءَتِ الْمُجَادِلَةُ تَشْتَكِي زَوْجَهَا إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم، وَأَنَا فِي جَنْبِ الْبَيْتِ، وَإِنَّهُ لَيَخْفَى عليَّ بَعْضُ كَلَامِهَا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿قَدْ سَمِعَ اللَّهُ قَوْلَ الَّتِي تُجَادِلُكَ فِي زَوْجِهَا وَتَشْتَكِي إِلَى اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ يَسْمَعُ تَحَاوُرَكُمَا إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَمِيعٌ بَصِيرٌ﴾ [الْمُجَادَلَةِ: ١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ هُوَ مُسْتَخْفٍ بِاللَّيْلِ﴾ أَيْ: مُخْتَفٍ فِي قَعْرِ بَيْتِهِ فِي ظَلَامِ اللَّيْلِ، ﴿وَسَارِبٌ بِالنَّهَارِ﴾ أَيْ: ظَاهِرٌ مَاشٍ فِي بَيَاضِ النَّهَارِ وَضِيَائِهِ، فَإِنَّ كِلَيْهِمَا فِي عِلْمِ اللَّهِ عَلَى السَّوَاءِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلا حِينَ يَسْتَغْشُونَ ثِيَابَهُمْ يَعْلَمُ مَا يُسِرُّونَ وَمَا يُعْلِنُونَ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٥] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا تَكُونُ فِي شَأْنٍ وَمَا تَتْلُو مِنْهُ مِنْ قُرْآنٍ وَلا تَعْمَلُونَ مِنْ عَمَلٍ إِلا كُنَّا عَلَيْكُمْ شُهُودًا إِذْ تُفِيضُونَ فِيهِ وَمَا يَعْزُبُ عَنْ رَبِّكَ مِنْ مِثْقَالِ ذَرَّةٍ فِي الأرْضِ وَلا فِي السَّمَاءِ وَلا أَصْغَرَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ وَلا أَكْبَرَ إِلا فِي كِتَابٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٦١] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: لِلْعَبْدِ مَلَائِكَةٌ يَتَعَاقَبُونَ عَلَيْهِ، حَرَس بِاللَّيْلِ وحَرَس بِالنَّهَارِ، يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنَ الْأَسْوَاءِ وَالْحَادِثَاتِ، كَمَا يَتَعَاقَبُ مَلَائِكَةٌ آخَرُونَ لِحِفْظِ الْأَعْمَالِ مِنْ خَيْرٍ أَوْ شَرٍّ، مَلَائِكَةٌ بِاللَّيْلِ وَمَلَائِكَةٌ بِالنَّهَارِ، فَاثْنَانِ عَنِ الْيَمِينِ و [عَنِ] الشِّمَالِ يَكْتُبَانِ الْأَعْمَالَ، صَاحِبُ الْيَمِينِ يَكْتُبُ الْحَسَنَاتِ، وَصَاحِبُ الشِّمَالِ يَكْتُبُ السَّيِّئَاتِ، وَمَلَكَانِ آخَرَانِ يَحْفَظَانِهِ وَيَحْرُسَانِهِ، وَاحِدًا مِنْ وَرَائِهِ وَآخِرَ مَنْ قُدَّامِهِ، فَهُوَ بَيْنُ أَرْبَعَةِ أَمْلَاكٍ بِالنَّهَارِ، وَأَرْبَعَةٍ آخَرِينَ بِاللَّيْلِ بَدَلًا حَافِظَانِ وَكَاتِبَانِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ: "يَتَعَاقَبُونَ فِيكُمْ مَلَائِكَةٌ بِاللَّيْلِ وَمَلَائِكَةٌ بِالنَّهَارِ، وَيَجْتَمِعُونَ فِي صَلَاةِ الصُّبْحِ وَصَلَاةِ الْعَصْرِ، فَيَصْعَدُ إِلَيْهِ الَّذِينَ بَاتُوا فِيكُمْ فَيَسْأَلُهُمْ وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بكم: كَيْفَ تَرَكْتُمْ عِبَادِي؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: أَتَيْنَاهُمْ وَهُمْ يُصَلُّونَ، وَتَرَكْنَاهُمْ وَهُمْ يُصَلُّونَ" وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "إِنَّ مَعَكُمْ مَنْ لَا يُفَارِقَكُمْ إِلَّا عِنْدَ الْخَلَاءِ وَعِنْدَ الْجِمَاعِ، فَاسْتَحْيُوهُمْ وَأَكْرِمُوهُمْ" .

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ وَالْمُعَقِّبَاتُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ، وَهِيَ الْمَلَائِكَةُ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: مَلَائِكَةٌ يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمَنْ خَلْفِهِ، فَإِذَا جَاءَ قَدَرُ اللَّهِ خَلَّوا عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: مَا مِنْ عَبْدٍ إِلَّا لَهُ مَلَك مُوَكَّلٌ، يَحْفَظُهُ فِي نَوْمِهِ وَيَقَظَتِهِ مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ وَالْهَوَامِّ، فَمَا مِنْهَا شَيْءٌ يَأْتِيهِ يُرِيدُهُ إِلَّا قَالَ الْمَلَكُ: وَرَاءَكَ إِلَّا شَيْءٌ يَأْذَنُ اللَّهُ فِيهِ فَيُصِيبُهُ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ عَنْ حَبِيبِ بْنِ أَبِي ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ﴾ قَالَ: ذَلِكَ مَلِكٌ مَنْ مُلُوكِ الدُّنْيَا، لَهُ حَرَسٌ مَنْ دُونِهِ حَرَسٌ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ﴾ يَعْنِي: وَلِيَّ الشَّيْطَانِ، يَكُونُ عَلَيْهِ الْحَرَسُ. وَقَالَ عِكْرِمة فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا: هَؤُلَاءِ الْأُمَرَاءُ: الْمَوَاكِبُ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمَنْ خَلْفِهِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ السُّلْطَانُ الْمُحْتَرِسُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ، وَهُمْ أَهْلُ الشِّرْكِ.

وَالظَّاهِرُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، أَنَّ مُرَاد ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وعِكْرِمة وَالضَّحَّاكِ بِهَذَا أَنَّ حَرْسَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ لِلْعَبِيدِ يُشْبِهُ حَرْسَ هَؤُلَاءِ لِمُلُوكِهِمْ وَأُمَرَائِهِمْ.

وَقَدْ روى الإمام أبو جعفر ابن جَرِيرٍ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثًا غَرِيبًا جِدًّا فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنِي الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ عَبْدِ السَّلَامِ بْنِ صَالِحٍ الْقُشَيْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْحَمِيدِ بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ كِنَانَةَ الْعَدَوِيِّ قَالَ: دَخَلَ عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عَفَّانَ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَخْبِرْنِي عَنِ الْعَبْدِ، كَمْ مَعَهُ مَنْ مَلَكٍ ؟ فَقَالَ: "مَلَكٌ عَلَى يَمِينِكَ عَلَى حَسَنَاتِكَ، وَهُوَ آمِرٌ عَلَى الَّذِي عَلَى الشِّمَالِ، إِذَا عَمِلْتَ حَسَنَةً كُتِبَتْ عَشْرًا، فَإِذَا عَمِلْتَ سَيِّئَةً قَالَ الَّذِي عَلَى الشِّمَالِ لِلَّذِي عَلَى الْيَمِينِ: أَكْتُبُ؟ قَالَ: لَا لَعَلَّهُ يَسْتَغْفِرُ اللَّهَ وَيَتُوبُ. فَإِذَا قَالَ ثلاثا قال: نَعَمْ، اكْتُبْ أَرَاحَنَا اللَّهُ مِنْهُ، فَبِئْسَ الْقَرِينُ. مَا أَقَلَّ مُرَاقَبَتَهُ لِلَّهِ وَأَقَلَّ اسْتِحْيَاءَهُ مِنَّا". يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿مَا يَلْفِظُ مِنْ قَوْلٍ إِلا لَدَيْهِ رَقِيبٌ عَتِيدٌ﴾ [ق: ١٨] وَمَلَكَانِ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْكَ وَمَنْ خَلْفِكَ، يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿لَهُ مُعَقِّبَاتٌ مِنْ بَيْنِ يَدَيْهِ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِ يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ وَمَلَكٌ قَابِضٌ عَلَى نَاصِيَتِكَ، فَإِذَا تَوَاضَعْتَ لِلَّهِ رَفَعَكَ، وَإِذَا تَجَبَّرْتَ عَلَى اللَّهِ قَصَمَكَ، وَمَلَكَانِ عَلَى شَفَتَيْكَ، لَيْسَ يَحْفَظَانِ عَلَيْكَ إِلَّا الصَّلَاةَ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ، وَمَلَكٌ قَائِمٌ عَلَى فِيكَ لَا يَدَع الْحَيَّةَ أَنَّ تَدَخُلَ فِي فِيكَ، وَمَلَكَانِ عَلَى عَيْنَيْكَ فَهَؤُلَاءِ عَشْرَةُ أَمْلَاكٍ عَلَى كُلِّ آدَمِيٍّ يَنْزِلُونَ مَلَائِكَةُ اللَّيْلِ عَلَى مَلَائِكَةِ النَّهَارِ؛ لِأَنَّ مَلَائِكَةَ اللَّيْلِ سِوَى مَلَائِكَةِ النَّهَارِ، فَهَؤُلَاءِ عِشْرُونَ مَلَكًا عَلَى كُلِّ آدَمِيٍّ وَإِبْلِيسُ بِالنَّهَارِ وَوَلَدُهُ بِاللَّيْلِ" .

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَسْوَدُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، حَدَّثَنِي مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ أَبِي الْجَعْدِ عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْكُمْ مِنْ أَحَدٍ إِلَّا وَقَدْ وُكِّلَ بِهِ قَرِينُهُ مِنَ الْجِنِّ وَقَرِينُهُ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ". قَالُوا: وَإِيَّاكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَالَ: "وَإِيَّايَ، وَلَكِنْ أَعَانَنِي اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ فَلَا يَأْمُرُنِي إِلَّا بِخَيْرٍ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ مُسْلِمٌ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ حفظُهم لَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ. رَوَاهُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، وَغَيْرُهُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ. وَإِلَيْهِ ذَهَبَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعي، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: وَفِي بَعْضِ الْقِرَاءَاتِ: "يَحْفَظُونَهُ بِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ".

وَقَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ: لَوْ تجلَّى لِابْنِ آدَمَ كُلُّ سَهْلٍ وَحَزَنٍ، لَرَأَى كُلَّ شَيْءٍ مِنْ ذَلِكَ شَيَاطِينَ لَوْلَا أَنَّ اللَّهَ وكَّل بِكُمْ مَلَائِكَةً عَنْكُمْ فِي مَطْعَمِكُمْ وَمَشْرَبِكُمْ وَعَوْرَاتِكُمْ، إِذًا لتُخُطّفتم.

وَقَالَ أَبُو أُمَامَةَ مَا مِنْ آدَمِيٍّ إِلَّا وَمَعَهُ مَلَكٌ يَذُود عَنْهُ، حَتَّى يُسْلِمَهُ لِلَّذِي قُدِّرَ لَهُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو مِجْلَز: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ مُرَاد إِلَى عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَهُوَ يُصَلِّي، فَقَالَ: احْتَرِسْ، فَإِنَّ نَاسًا مِنْ مُرَادٍ يُرِيدُونَ قَتْلَكَ. فَقَالَ: إِنْ مَعَ كُلِّ رَجُلٍ مَلَكَيْنِ يَحْفَظَانِهِ مِمَّا لَمْ يُقَدَّرْ، فَإِذَا جَاءَ القَدَرُ خَليا بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهُ، وَإِنَّ الْأَجَلَ جُنَّةٌ حَصِينة. 

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: ﴿يَحْفَظُونَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ بِأَمْرِ اللَّهِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَرَأَيْتَ رُقَى نَسْتَرْقِي بِهَا، هَلْ تَرُدُّ مَنْ قَدَر اللَّهِ شَيْئًا؟ فَقَالَ: "هِيَ مَنْ قَدَر الله" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْأَشَجُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ غِيَاثٍ، عَنْ أَشْعَثَ، عَنْ جَهْم، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ قَالَ: أَوْحَى اللَّهُ إِلَى نَبِيٍّ مِنْ أَنْبِيَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ: أَنْ قُلْ لِقَوْمِكَ: إِنَّهُ لَيْسَ مِنْ أَهْلِ قَرْيَةٍ وَلَا أَهْلِ بَيْتٍ يَكُونُونَ عَلَى طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ فَيَتَحَوَّلُونَ مِنْهَا إِلَى مَعْصِيَةِ اللَّهِ، إِلَّا تَحَوَّلَ لَهُمْ مِمَّا يُحِبُّونَ إِلَى مَا يَكْرَهُونَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: إِنَّ مِصْدَاقَ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُغَيِّرُ مَا بِقَوْمٍ حَتَّى يُغَيِّرُوا مَا بِأَنْفُسِهِمْ﴾

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ هَذَا فِي حَدِيثٍ مَرْفُوعٍ، فَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ بْنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ فِي كِتَابِهِ "صِفَةُ الْعَرْشِ": حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، حَدَّثَنَا الْهَيْثَمُ بْنُ الْأَشْعَثِ السُّلَمِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو حَنِيفَةَ الْيَمَامِيُّ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنْ عُمَيْرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: خَطَبَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ عَلَى مِنْبَرِ الْكُوفَةِ، قَالَ: كُنْتُ إِذَا سكتُّ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ ابْتَدَأَنِي، وَإِذَا سَأَلْتُهُ عَنِ الْخَبَرِ أَنْبَأَنِي، وَإِنَّهُ حَدَّثَنِي عَنْ رَبِّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، قَالَ: "قَالَ الرَّبُّ: وَعِزَّتِي وَجَلَالِي، وَارْتِفَاعِي فَوْقَ عَرْشِي، مَا مِنْ أَهْلِ قَرْيَةٍ وَلَا أَهْلِ بَيْتٍ كَانُوا عَلَى مَا كرهتُ مِنْ مَعْصِيَتِي، ثُمَّ تَحَوَّلُوا عَنْهَا إِلَى مَا أَحْبَبْتُ مِنْ طَاعَتِي، إِلَّا تَحَوَّلْتُ لَهُمْ عَمَّا يَكْرَهُونَ مِنْ عَذَابِي إِلَى مَا يُحِبُّونَ مِنْ رَحْمَتِي" .

وَهَذَا غَرِيبٌ، وَفِي إِسْنَادِهِ مَنْ لَا أَعْرِفُهُ.

---

## 13:12-13 — verses 12-13 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs that He is the One who subjects lightning, which is what is seen as the flashing light gleaming through the gaps of the clouds.

Ibn Jarir related that Ibn Abbas wrote to Abu al-Jald asking him about lightning, and he said: lightning is water.

Regarding His saying, {in fear and hope}: Qatadah said, in fear for the traveler, who fears its harm and the difficulty it brings, and in hope for the resident, who hopes for its blessing and benefit and hopes for God's provision.

{And He produces the heavy clouds}, meaning He creates them newly formed, and they are heavy, close to the earth, because of the abundance of water in them.

Mujahid said: the heavy clouds are those that contain water.

{And the thunder glorifies Him with praise}, as the Almighty said, {And there is not a thing except that it glorifies Him with praise} [al-Isra: 44].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ibrahim ibn Sa'd said, my father informed me, saying: I was sitting beside Humayd ibn Abd al-Rahman in the mosque, when an old man from Banu Ghifar passed by. Humayd sent for him, and when he came he said: O son of my brother, make room for him between me and you, for he accompanied the Messenger of God ﷺ. So he came and sat between me and him, and Humayd said to him: What is the hadith you told me from the Messenger of God ﷺ? The old man said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say, "Indeed God brings forth the clouds, and they speak with the best speech, and laugh with the best laughter."

The meaning, and God knows best, is that their speech is thunder and their laughter is lightning.

Musa ibn Ubaydah said, from Sa'd ibn Ibrahim, who said: God sends forth the rain, and there is nothing more beautiful in its laughter, nor more pleasant in its speech, for its laughter is the lightning and its speech is the thunder.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Muslim said: It has reached us that lightning is an angel with four faces: the face of a human, the face of an ox, the face of an eagle, and the face of a lion, and when he strikes with his tail, that is the lightning.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Salim, from his father, said: When the Messenger of God ﷺ heard thunder and thunderbolts, he would say, "O God, do not kill us with Your wrath, and do not destroy us with Your punishment, and grant us well-being before that."

Al-Tirmidhi related it, and al-Bukhari in the Book of Manners, and al-Nasa'i in al-Yawm wa'l-Layla, and al-Hakim in his Mustadrak, from the hadith of al-Hajjaj ibn Artah, from Abu Matar, whose name was not given.

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] a man, from Abu Hurayrah, raised the hadith, saying: Whenever he heard thunder he would say, "Glory be to the One whom the thunder glorifies with praise."

It was related from Ali, may God be pleased with him, that when he heard the sound of thunder he would say: Glory be to the One for whom it glorifies.

Likewise it was related from Ibn Abbas, al-Aswad ibn Yazid, and Tawus, that they used to say the same.

Al-Awza'i said: Ibn Abi Zakariyya used to say: Whoever says, when he hears thunder, "Glory be to God and praise be to Him," will not be struck by a thunderbolt.

And from Abdullah ibn al-Zubayr, that when he heard thunder he would stop speaking and say: Glory be to the One whom the thunder glorifies with praise, and the angels out of fear of Him, and he would say: This is indeed a severe warning to the people of the earth. Malik related it in al-Muwatta, and al-Bukhari in the Book of Manners.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah reported that the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Your Lord, Mighty and Majestic, said: If My servants obeyed Me, I would give them rain by night, and cause the sun to rise upon them by day, and I would not let them hear the sound of thunder."

Al-Tabarani said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "When you hear thunder, remember God, for it does not strike one who remembers Him."

Regarding His saying, {And He sends thunderbolts, striking with them whom He wills}, meaning He sends them as a punishment by which He takes vengeance upon whom He wills. For this reason they increase at the end of time, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may God be pleased with him, reported that the Prophet ﷺ said, "Thunderbolts will increase as the Hour draws near, until a man comes to a people and says: Who was struck by a thunderbolt this morning? And they say: So-and-so, and so-and-so, and so-and-so were struck."

It has been related regarding the reason for its revelation what the Hafiz Abu Ya'la al-Mawsili reported:

[chain] Anas reported that the Messenger of God ﷺ once sent a man to a man among the tyrants of the Arabs, saying, "Go and call him to me." He said: So he went to him and said: The Messenger of God calls you. He said to him: Who is the Messenger of God? And what is God? Is He of gold, or of silver, or of copper? He said: So he returned to the Messenger of God ﷺ and told him. He said: O Messenger of God, I told you he is more insolent than that, he said such and such to me. He said, "Return to him a second time." I think he went, and he said the same to him. So he returned to the Messenger of God, may God's peace and blessings be upon him, and said: O Messenger of God, I told you he is more insolent than that. He said, "Return to him and call him again." So he returned to him a third time. He said: He repeated the same speech to him. And while he was speaking to him, God, Mighty and Majestic, sent a cloud directly over his head, and it thundered, and a thunderbolt fell from it, and it took off the top of his skull. Then God revealed: {And He sends thunderbolts, striking with them whom He wills, while they dispute concerning God, and He is severe in contriving}.

Ibn Jarir related it from the hadith of Ali ibn Abi Sarah, with this chain. The Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar related it from Abdah ibn Abdullah, from Yazid ibn Harun, from Daylam ibn Ghazwan, from Thabit, from Anas, mentioning something similar.

He also said: [chain] Abd al-Rahman ibn Suhar al-Abdi reported that it reached him that the Prophet of God sent him to a tyrant to call him, and he said: Tell me about your Lord, is He gold, or silver, or pearl? He said: And while he was disputing with them, God sent a cloud, and it thundered, and He sent down upon him a thunderbolt that took off the top of his skull, and this verse was revealed.

Abu Bakr ibn Ayyash said, from Layth ibn Abi Sulaym, from Mujahid, who said: A Jew came and said: O Muhammad, tell me about your Lord, of what is He? Is He of copper? Of pearl? Or of ruby? He said: So a thunderbolt came and seized him, and God revealed: {And He sends thunderbolts, striking with them whom He wills}.

Qatadah said: It was mentioned to us that a man denied the Qur'an and disbelieved the Prophet ﷺ, so God sent a thunderbolt that destroyed him, and He revealed: {And He sends thunderbolts...} to the end of the verse.

They also mentioned, as a reason for its revelation, the story of Amir ibn al-Tufayl and Arbad ibn Rabi'ah when they came to the Messenger of God ﷺ in Medina and asked him to grant them half of authority, but the Messenger of God ﷺ refused them. Amir ibn al-Tufayl, may God curse him, said to him: By God, I will surely fill it against you with swift horses and beardless young men. The Messenger of God ﷺ said to him: God refuses you that, and so do the sons of Qaylah, meaning the Ansar. Then the two of them intended to assassinate the Prophet ﷺ, and one of them began speaking to him while the other drew his sword to kill him from behind. But God protected him from them and preserved him. So they left Medina and went out among the tribes of the Arabs, gathering people to fight him, peace be upon him. Then God sent upon Arbad a cloud containing a thunderbolt that burned him. As for Amir ibn al-Tufayl, God sent plague upon him, and a great swelling appeared on him, and he began to say: O family of Amir, a swelling like the swelling of a young camel, and death in the house of a woman of Sulul? Until the two of them died, may God curse them. And God revealed concerning the like of that: {And He sends thunderbolts, striking with them whom He wills}. Concerning this, Labid ibn Rabi'ah, the brother of Arbad, said in his elegy for him:

I fear for Arbad the various forms of death, but I do not fear the setting of al-Simak and the constellation of Leo...

Thunder and thunderbolts afflicted me with...

"A rider on the day of harsh battle, the stout-hearted one."

Al-Hafiz Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] Ibn Abbas reported that Arbad ibn Qays ibn Jaz' ibn Julayd ibn Ja'far ibn Kilab, and Amir ibn al-Tufayl ibn Malik, came to Medina to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ. They came to him while he was sitting, and they sat before him. Amir ibn al-Tufayl said: "O Muhammad, what will you grant me if I become Muslim?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "You will have what the Muslims have, and you will bear what they bear." Amir ibn al-Tufayl said: "Will you grant me authority after you if I become Muslim?" The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "That is not for you, nor for your people, but you may have command of the cavalry." He said: "I already command the cavalry of Najd. Grant me the tent-dwellers and you keep the town-dwellers." The Messenger of Allah said: "No."

When the two of them turned away from him, Amir said: "By Allah, I will surely fill this land against you with horsemen and men." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to him: "Allah will prevent you."
