When Arbad and Amir went out, Amir said: "O Arbad, I will occupy Muhammad ﷺ with conversation, so strike him with the sword. For if you kill Muhammad, the people will not go beyond accepting blood money and disliking war, and we will pay them the blood money." Arbad said: "I will do it."

So the two of them came back to him. Amir said: "O Muhammad, stand with me, I wish to speak with you." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood with him, and the two of them sat by the wall, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood speaking with him. Arbad drew his sword, but when he placed his hand upon it, his hand stuck fast to the hilt of the sword, and he was unable to draw it. So Arbad delayed in striking, as Amir had asked. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ turned and saw Arbad and what he was doing, and he turned away from them both.

When Amir and Arbad left the presence of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and when they reached the lava plain, the Harra of Waqim, they stopped there. Sa'd ibn Mu'adh and Usayd ibn Hudayr came out to them and said: "Be gone, you two enemies of Allah, may Allah curse you." Amir said: "Who is this, O Sa'd?" He said: "This is Usayd ibn Hudayr of the war bands."

The two of them went on until, when they reached al-Raqm, Allah sent down a thunderbolt upon Arbad which killed him. Amir went on until, when he reached al-Kharim, Allah sent an abscess which afflicted him, and night overtook him in the house of a woman of the Banu Salul. He kept touching the abscess on his throat, saying: "A swelling like the swelling of a camel, in the house of a woman of Salul! Does she wish that I die in her house?" Then he mounted his horse and rode it hard until he died upon it while returning.

Then Allah revealed concerning the two of them: {Allah knows what every female carries and what the wombs diminish} up to His saying {and they have no protector besides Him} [al-Ra'd 13:8-11]. He said: the succeeding angels by the command of Allah guard Muhammad ﷺ. Then He mentioned Arbad and what killed him, saying: {And He sends the thunderbolts and strikes with them whom He wills} the rest of the verse.

Concerning His saying, {while they dispute concerning Allah}, that is, they doubt His greatness, and that there is no god but He. {And He is severe in al-Mihal (contention/retribution)}.

Ibn Jarir said: severe is His retribution in punishing whoever transgresses against Him, becomes insolent, and persists in his disbelief.

This verse resembles His saying: {And they plotted a plot, and We planned a plan, while they perceived it not. So see how was the end of their plotting: We destroyed them and their people, all together} [al-Naml 27:50-51].

And it is reported from Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, concerning {And He is severe in al-Mihal}: that is, severe in seizing. Mujahid said: severe in strength.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي يُسَخِّرُ الْبَرْقَ، وَهُوَ مَا يُرَى مِنَ النُّورِ اللَّامِعِ سَاطِعًا مِنْ خِلَلِ السَّحَابِ.

وَرَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ كَتَبَ إِلَى أَبِي الْجَلْدِ يَسْأَلُهُ عَنِ الْبَرْقِ، فَقَالَ: الْبَرْقُ: الْمَاءُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿خَوْفًا وَطَمَعًا﴾ قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: خَوْفًا لِلْمُسَافِرِ، يَخَافُ أَذَاهُ وَمَشَقَّتَهُ، وَطَمَعًا لِلْمُقِيمِ يَرْجُو بَرَكَتَهُ وَمَنْفَعَتَهُ، وَيَطْمَعُ فِي رِزْقِ اللَّهِ.

﴿وَيُنْشِئُ السَّحَابَ الثِّقَالَ﴾ أَيْ: وَيَخْلُقُهَا مُنْشَأَةً جَدِيدَةً، وَهِيَ لِكَثْرَةِ مَائِهَا ثَقِيلَةٌ قَرِيبَةٌ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: والسحاب الثقال: الذي فيه الماء.

﴿وَيُسَبِّحُ الرَّعْدُ بِحَمْدِهِ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِلا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٤٤] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي أَبِي قَالَ: كُنْتُ جَالِسًا إِلَى جَنْبِ حُمَيْد بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ، فَمَرَّ شَيْخٌ مِنْ بَنِي غِفَارٍ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَيْهِ حُمَيْدٌ، فَلَمَّا أَقْبَلَ قَالَ: يَا ابْنَ أَخِي، وَسِّعْ لَهُ فِيمَا بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكَ، فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ صَحِبَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَجَاءَ حَتَّى جَلَسَ فِيمَا بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَهُ، فَقَالَ لَهُ حُمَيْدٌ: مَا الْحَدِيثُ الَّذِي حَدَّثْتَنِي عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ فقال الشَّيْخُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُنْشِئُ السَّحَابَ، فَيَنْطِقُ أَحْسَنَ النُّطْقِ، وَيَضْحَكُ أَحْسَنَ الضَّحِكِ" .

وَالْمُرَادُ -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -أَنَّ نطقَها الرعدُ، وَضَحِكَهَا البرقُ.

وَقَالَ مُوسَى بْنُ عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ سَعْدِ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ قَالَ: يَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ الْغَيْثَ، فَلَا أَحْسَنَ مِنْهُ مَضْحَكًا، وَلَا آنَسَ مِنْهُ مَنْطِقًا، فَضَحِكُهُ الْبَرْقُ، وَمَنْطِقُهُ الرَّعْدُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ الرَّازِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ قَالَ: بَلَغَنَا أَنَّ الْبَرْقَ مَلكٌ لَهُ أَرْبَعَةُ وُجُوهٍ: وَجْهُ إِنْسَانٍ، وَوَجْهُ ثَوْرٍ، وَوَجْهُ نَسْرٍ، وَوَجْهُ أَسَدٍ، فَإِذَا مَصَع بِذَنَبِهِ فَذَاكَ الْبَرْقُ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْوَاحِدِ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَجَّاجُ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو مَطَرٍ، عَنْ سَالِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا سَمع الرعْد وَالصَّوَاعِقَ قَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ، لَا تَقْتُلْنَا بِغَضَبِكَ، وَلَا تُهْلِكْنَا بِعَذَابِكَ، وَعَافِنَا قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ".

وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالْبُخَارِيُّ فِي كِتَابِ الْأَدَبِ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةِ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِي مُسْتَدْرَكِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْحَجَّاجِ بْنِ أَرَطَاةَ، عَنْ أَبِي مَطَرٍ -وَلَمْ يُسَمَّ بِهِ. 

وَقَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أَحْمَدَ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَفَعَ الْحَدِيثَ قَالَ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ إِذَا سَمِعَ الرَّعْدَ قَالَ: "سُبْحَانَ مَنْ يُسبّح الرعْد بِحَمْدِهِ". 

وَرُوِيَ عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّهُ كَانَ إِذَا سَمِعَ صَوْتَ الرَّعْدِ قَالَ: سبحان من سَبَّحت له.

وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالْأَسْوَدِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ، وَطَاوُسٍ: أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَقُولُونَ كَذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ: كَانَ ابْنُ أَبِي زَكَرِيَّا يَقُولُ: مَنْ قَالَ حِينَ يَسْمَعُ الرَّعْدَ: سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ وَبِحَمْدِهِ، لَمْ تُصِبْهُ صَاعِقَةٌ.

وَعَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ أَنَّهُ كَانَ إِذَا سَمِعَ الرَّعْدَ تَرَكَ الْحَدِيثَ وَقَالَ: سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي يُسَبِّحُ الرعدُ بِحَمْدِهِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ مِنْ خِيفَتِهِ، وَيَقُولُ: إِنَّ هَذَا لَوَعِيدٌ شديدٌ لِأَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ. رَوَاهُ مَالِكٌ فِي الْمُوَطَّأِ، وَالْبُخَارِيِّ فِي كِتَابِ الْأَدَبِ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا صَدَقة بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ وَاسِعٍ، عَنْ شتيز بْنِ نَهَارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: لَوْ أَنَّ عَبِيدِي أَطَاعُونِي لَأَسْقَيْتُهُمُ الْمَطَرَ بِاللَّيْلِ، وَأَطْلَعْتُ عَلَيْهِمُ الشَّمْسَ بِالنَّهَارِ، وَلَمَا أَسْمَعْتُهُمْ صَوْتَ الرَّعْدِ". 

وَقَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا زَكَرِيَّا بْنُ يَحْيَى السَّاجِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كَامِلٍ الجَحْدري، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ كَثِيرٍ أَبُو النَّضْرِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْكَرِيمِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا سَمِعْتُمُ الرَّعْدَ فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ؛ فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُصِيبُ ذَاكِرًا". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ فَيُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ أَيْ: يُرْسِلُهَا نقمَةً يَنْتَقِمُ بِهَا مِمَّنْ يَشَاءُ، وَلِهَذَا تَكْثُرُ فِي آخِرِ الزَّمَانِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ مُصْعَبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَارَةُ عَنْ أَبِي نَضْرَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ؛ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "تَكْثُرُ الصَّوَاعِقُ عِنْدَ اقْتِرَابِ السَّاعَةِ، حَتَّى يَأْتِيَ الرَّجُلُ الْقَوْمَ فَيَقُولُ: مَنْ صُعِقَ تِلْكُمُ الْغَدَاةَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ صعِق فُلَانٌ وَفُلَانٌ وَفُلَانٌ". 

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ فِي سَبَبِ نُزُولِهَا مَا رَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى الْمُوصِلِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي سَارَّةَ الشَّيباني، حَدَّثَنَا ثَابِتٌ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَعَثَ رَجُلًا مَرَّةً إِلَى رَجُلٍ مِنْ فَرَاعِنَةِ الْعَرَبِ فَقَالَ: "اذْهَبْ فَادْعُهُ لِي". قَالَ: فَذَهَبَ إِلَيْهِ فَقَالَ: يَدْعُوكَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ. فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَنْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ؟ وَمَا اللَّهُ؟ أمِن ذَهَبٍ هُوَ؟ أَمْ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ هُوَ؟ أَمْ مِنْ نُحَاسٍ هُوَ؟ قَالَ: فَرَجَعَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَأَخْبَرَهُ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قد أخبرتك أنه أعتى من ذلك، قَالَ لِي كَذَا وَكَذَا. فَقَالَ: "ارْجِعْ إِلَيْهِ الثَّانِيَةَ". أُرَاهُ، فَذَهَبَ فَقَالَ لَهُ مِثْلَهَا. فَرَجَعَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَدْ أَخْبَرْتُكَ أَنَّهُ أَعْتَى مِنْ ذَلِكَ. قَالَ: "ارْجِعْ إِلَيْهِ فَادْعُهُ". فَرَجَعَ إِلَيْهِ الثَّالِثَةَ. قَالَ: فَأَعَادَ عَلَيْهِ ذَلِكَ الْكَلَامَ. فَبَيْنَا هُوَ يُكَلِّمُهُ، إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، سَحَابَةً حِيَالَ رَأْسِهِ، فَرَعَدَتْ، فَوَقَعَتْ مِنْهَا صَاعِقَةٌ، فَذَهَبَ بِقِحْفِ رَأْسِهِ فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ فَيُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَهُمْ يُجَادِلُونَ فِي اللَّهِ وَهُوَ شَدِيدُ الْمِحَالِ﴾

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنَ جَرِيرٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي سَارَّةَ، بِهِ وَرَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ، عَنْ عَبْدَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، عَنْ دَيْلَمِ بْنِ غَزْوان، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ. 

وَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبَانُ بن يزيد، حدثنا أبو عمران الجوقي، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ صُحَار الْعَبْدِيِّ: أَنَّهُ بَلَغَهُ أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ بَعَثَهُ إِلَى جَبَّار يَدْعُوهُ، فَقَالَ: أَرَأَيْتُمْ رَبَّكُمْ، أَذَهَبٌ هُوَ؟ أَوْ فِضَّةٌ هُوَ؟ أَلُؤْلُؤٌ هُوَ؟ قَالَ: فَبَيْنَا هُوَ يُجَادِلُهُمْ، إِذْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ سَحَابَةً فَرَعَدَتْ فَأَرْسَلَ عَلَيْهِ صَاعِقَةً فَذَهَبَتْ بِقِحْفِ رَأْسِهِ، وَنَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ لَيْثِ بْنِ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ يَهُودِيٌّ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَخْبِرْنِي عَنْ رَبِّكَ، [مِنْ أَيِّ شَيْءٍ هُوَ] مِنْ نُحَاسٍ هُوَ؟ مَنْ لُؤْلُؤٍ؟ أَوْ يَاقُوتٍ؟ قَالَ: فَجَاءَتْ صَاعِقَةٌ فَأَخَذَتْهُ، وأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ فَيُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ذُكر لَنَا أنَّ رَجُلًا أَنْكَرَ الْقُرْآنَ، وَكَذَّبَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ صَاعِقَةً فَأَهْلَكَتْهُ وأَنْزَلَ: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَذَكَرُوا فِي سَبَبِ نُزُولِهَا قِصَّةَ عَامِرِ بْنِ الطُّفَيْلِ وَأَرْبَدَ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ لَمَّا قَدِمَا عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الْمَدِينَةَ، فَسَأَلَاهُ أَنْ يَجْعَلَ لَهُمَا نِصْفَ الْأَمْرِ فَأَبَى عَلَيْهِمَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَقَالَ لَهُ عَامِرُ بْنُ الطُّفَيْلِ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ: أَمَا وَاللَّهِ لأملأنَّهَا عَلَيْكَ خَيْلًا جَرْدا وَرِجَالًا مُرْدًا. فَقَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: يَأْبَى اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ ذَلِكَ وَأَبْنَاءُ قَيْلة يَعْنِي: الْأَنْصَارَ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُمَا هَمَّا بِالْفَتْكِ بِالنَّبِيِّ ﷺ، وَجَعَلَ أَحَدُهُمَا يُخَاطِبُهُ، وَالْآخَرُ يَسْتَلُّ سَيْفَهُ لِيَقْتُلَهُ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ، فَحَمَاهُ اللَّهُ مِنْهُمَا وَعَصَمَهُ، فَخَرَجَا مِنَ الْمَدِينَةِ فَانْطَلَقَا فِي أَحْيَاءِ الْعَرَبِ، يَجْمَعَانِ النَّاسَ لِحَرْبِهِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أَرْبَدَ سَحَابَةً فِيهَا صَاعِقَةٌ فَأَحْرَقَتْهُ. وَأَمَّا عَامِرُ بْنُ الطُّفَيْلِ فَأَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الطَّاعُونَ، فَخَرَجَتْ فِيهِ غُدّة عَظِيمَةٌ، فَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ: يَا آلَ عَامِرٍ، غُدَّة كغدَّة الْبِكْرِ، وَمَوْتٌ فِي بَيْتِ سَلُولية ؟ حَتَّى مَاتَا لَعَنَهُمَا اللَّهُ، وأنزل الله في مثل ذلك: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ فَيُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ وَفِي ذَلِكَ يَقُولُ لَبِيدُ بْنُ رَبِيعَةَ، أَخُو أَرْبَدَ يَرْثِيهِ:

أخشَى عَلَى أَرْبَدَ الحُتُوفَ وَلا ... أرْهَب نَوء السِّمَاكِ والأسَد ...

فَجَعني الرّعْدُ والصّواعِقُ بِالْـ ... فَارِسِ يَوم الكريهَة النَّجُدِ 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مَسْعَدة بْنُ سَعْدٍ الْعَطَّارُ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ الْحِزَامِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ عِمْرَانَ، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ ابْنَا زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِمَا، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، أَنَّ أَرْبَدَ بْنَ قَيْسِ بْنِ جَزْء بْنِ جُلَيْدِ بْنِ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ كِلَابٍ، وَعَامِرَ بْنَ الطُّفَيْلِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ، قَدِمَا الْمَدِينَةِ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَانْتَهَيَا إِلَيْهِ وَهُوَ جَالِسٌ، فَجَلَسَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، فَقَالَ عَامِرُ بْنُ الطُّفَيْلِ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، مَا تَجْعَلُ لِي إِنْ أسلمتُ؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَكَ مَا لِلْمُسْلِمِينَ، وَعَلَيْكَ مَا عَلَيْهِمْ". قَالَ عَامِرُ بْنُ الطُّفَيْلِ: أَتَجْعَلُ لِيَ الْأَمْرَ إِنْ أَسْلَمْتُ مَنْ بَعْدِكَ؟ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَيْسَ ذَلِكَ لَكَ وَلَا لِقَوْمِكَ، وَلَكِنَّ لَكَ أعنَّة الْخَيْلِ". قَالَ: أَنَا الْآنَ فِي أعنَّة خَيْلِ نَجِدٍ، اجْعَلْ لِيَ الوبَرَ وَلَكَ المدَرَ. قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ: "لَا". فَلَمَّا قَفَلَا مِنْ عِنْدِهِ قَالَ عَامِرٌ: أَمَا وَاللَّهِ لأملأنَّهَا عَلَيْكَ خَيْلًا وَرِجَالًا فَقَالَ لَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَمْنَعُكَ اللَّهُ". فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ أَرْبَدُ وَعَامِرٌ، قَالَ عَامِرٌ: يَا أَرْبَدُ، أَنَا أَشْغَلُ عَنْكَ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ بِالْحَدِيثِ، فَاضْرِبْهُ بِالسَّيْفِ، فَإِنَّ النَّاسَ إِذَا قَتَلْتَ مُحَمَّدًا لَمْ يَزِيدُوا عَلَى أَنْ يَرضَوا بِالدِّيَةِ، وَيَكْرَهُوا الْحَرْبَ، فَنُعْطِيهِمُ الدِّيَةَ. قَالَ أَرْبَدُ: أَفْعَلُ. فَأَقْبَلَا رَاجِعِينَ إِلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ عَامِرٌ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، قُمْ مَعِي أُكَلِّمُكَ. فَقَامَ مَعَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَجَلَسَا إِلَى الْجِدَارِ، وَوَقَفَ مَعَهُ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُكَلِّمُهُ، وسَلّ أربدُ السَّيْفَ، فَلَمَّا وَضَعَ يَدَهُ عَلَى السَّيْفِ يَبِسَتْ يَدُهُ عَلَى قَائِمِ السَّيْفِ، فَلَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ سَلَّ السَّيْفِ، فَأَبْطَأَ أَرْبَدُ عَلَى عَامِرٍ بِالضَّرْبِ، فَالْتَفَتَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَرَأَى أَرْبَدَ، وَمَا يَصْنَعُ، فَانْصَرَفَ عَنْهُمَا. فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ عَامِرٌ وَأَرْبَدُ مِنْ عِنْدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَا بالحَرّة، حَرّة وَاقِمٍ نَزَلَا فَخَرَجَ إِلَيْهِمَا سَعْدُ بْنُ مُعَاذٍ وأسَيد بْنُ حُضَيْرٍ فَقَالَا اشْخَصَا يَا عَدُوَّيِ اللَّهِ، لَعَنَكُمَا اللَّهُ. فَقَالَ عَامِرٌ: مَنْ هَذَا يَا سَعْدُ؟ قَالَ: هَذَا أسَيد بْنُ حُضَير الْكَتَائِبِ فَخَرَجَا حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَا بالرَّقم، أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أربدَ صَاعِقَةً فَقَتَلَتْهُ، وَخَرَجَ عَامِرٌ حَتَّى إِذَا كَانَ بِالْخَرِيمِ، أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ قُرْحَةً فَأَخَذَتْهُ فَأَدْرَكَهُ اللَّيْلُ فِي بَيْتِ امْرَأَةٍ مِنْ بَنِي سَلُولٍ، فَجَعَلَ يَمَسُّ قُرْحَتَهُ فِي حَلْقِهِ وَيَقُولُ: غُدَّةٌ كَغُدَّةِ الْجَمَلِ فِي بَيْتِ سَلُولية تَرْغَبُ أَنْ يَمُوتَ فِي بَيْتِهَا! ثُمَّ رَكِبَ فَرَسَهُ فَأُحْضِرَهُ حَتَّى مَاتَ عَلَيْهِ رَاجِعًا، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمَا: ﴿اللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ مَا تَحْمِلُ كُلُّ أُنْثَى وَمَا تَغِيضُ الأرْحَامُ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِهِ مِنْ وَالٍ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٨ -١١]-قَالَ: الْمُعَقِّبَاتُ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ يَحْفَظُونَ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ، ثُمَّ ذَكَّرَ أَرْبَدَ وَمَا قَتَلَهُ بِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَيُرْسِلُ الصَّوَاعِقَ فَيُصِيبُ بِهَا مَنْ يَشَاءُ﴾ الآية .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَهُمْ يُجَادِلُونَ فِي اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: يَشُكّون فِي عَظَمَتِهِ، وَأَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، ﴿وَهُوَ شَدِيدُ الْمِحَالِ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: شَدِيدَةٌ مماحَلَته فِي عُقُوبَةِ مَنْ طَغَى عَلَيْهِ وَعَتَا وَتَمَادَى فِي كُفْرِهِ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ شَبِيهَةٌ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَكَرُوا مَكْرًا وَمَكَرْنَا مَكْرًا وَهُمْ لَا يَشْعُرُونَ فَانْظُرْ كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ مَكْرِهِمْ أَنَّا دَمَّرْنَاهُمْ وَقَوْمَهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ٥٠، ٥١] .

وَعَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: ﴿وَهُوَ شَدِيدُ الْمِحَالِ﴾ أَيْ: شَدِيدُ الْأَخْذِ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: شَدِيدُ الْقُوَّةِ.

---

## 13:14 — verse 14

### Translation

'Ali ibn Abi Talib, may Allah be pleased with him, said concerning {His is the call of truth}: "This means monotheism (al-tawhid)." Ibn Jarir related it.

Ibn 'Abbas, Qatadah, and Malik, from Muhammad ibn al-Munkadir, said concerning {His is the call of truth}: "It means, there is no god but Allah."

{And those whom they call upon besides Him}, meaning: the likeness of those who worship gods other than Allah. {is like one who stretches out his two hands toward water so that it may reach his mouth, but it does not reach it}. 'Ali ibn Abi Talib said: "It is like the likeness of one who reaches for water at the edge of a well with his hand, yet he can never attain it with his hand, so how then could it reach his mouth?"

Mujahid said concerning {like one who stretches out his two hands}: "He calls to the water with his tongue and gestures toward it with his hand, but it never comes to him."

It has also been said that what is meant is like one who closes his hand upon water, for he cannot hold on to any of it, just as the poet said:

"Indeed I, and you, and my longing for you, are like one who grasps water that his fingers cannot retain."

And another poet said:

"So I became, regarding what had been between her and me of affection, like one who grasps water in his hand."

The meaning of the passage is: this one who stretches out his hand toward the water, whether closing his hand upon it or reaching for it from a distance, just as he derives no benefit from water that does not reach his mouth, the place appointed for drinking, so too these polytheists who worship, besides Allah, a god other than Him, will never derive any benefit from them, neither in this world nor in the Hereafter. That is why He said: {And the calling of the disbelievers is nothing but error}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: ﴿لَهُ دَعْوَةُ الْحَقِّ﴾ قَالَ: التَّوْحِيدُ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَمَالكٌ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ المنْكَدِر: ﴿لَهُ دَعْوَةُ الْحَقِّ﴾ [قَالَ] لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ.

﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَثَلُ الَّذِينَ يَعْبُدُونَ آلِهَةً غَيْرَ اللَّهِ. ﴿كَبَاسِطِ كَفَّيْهِ إِلَى الْمَاءِ لِيَبْلُغَ فَاهُ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ: كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي يَتَنَاوَلُ الْمَاءَ مِنْ طَرَفِ الْبِئْرِ بِيَدِهِ، وَهُوَ لَا يَنَالُهُ أَبَدًا بِيَدِهِ، فَكَيْفَ يَبْلُغُ فَاهُ؟.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿كَبَاسِطِ كَفَّيْهِ﴾ يَدْعُو الْمَاءَ بِلِسَانِهِ، وَيُشِيرُ إِلَيْهِ [بِيَدِهِ] فَلَا يَأْتِيهِ أَبَدًا.

وَقِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ كَقَابِضِ يَدَهُ عَلَى الْمَاءِ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُحْكِمُ مِنْهُ عَلَى شَيْءٍ، كَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ: 

فَإنّي وَإيَّاكُمْ وَشَوْقًا إليكمُ ... كَقَابض مَاء لَم تَسْقه أناملُه ...

وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ: 

فأصْبَحتُ ممَّا كانَ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَها ... مِن الوُدّ مِثْلَ القابضِ المَاءَ بِاليَد ...

وَمَعْنَى الْكَلَامِ: أَنَّ هَذَا الَّذِي يَبْسُطُ يَدَهُ إِلَى الْمَاءِ، إِمَّا قَابِضًا وَإِمَّا مُتَنَاوِلًا له من بُعد، كما أنه لا يَنْتَفِعُ بِالْمَاءِ الَّذِي لَمْ يَصِلْ إِلَى فِيهِ، الَّذِي جَعَلَهُ مَحَلًّا لِلشُّرْبِ، فَكَذَلِكَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ الَّذِينَ يَعْبُدُونَ مَعَ اللَّهِ إِلَهًا غَيْرَهُ، لَا يَنْتَفِعُونَ بِهِمْ أَبَدًا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَلَا فِي الْآخِرَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا دُعَاءُ الْكَافِرِينَ إِلا فِي ضَلالٍ﴾

---

## 13:15 — verse 15

### Translation

He, the Exalted, informs us of His greatness and His dominion which has overpowered everything, and to which everything has submitted. This is why everything prostrates to Him: willingly from the believers, and unwillingly from the polytheists. {And their shadows in the mornings} means at daybreak, {and the evenings}, which is the plural of asil, referring to the latter part of the day, as He, the Exalted, said: {Have they not looked at whatever thing Allah has created, how its shadows incline to the right and to the left, prostrating to Allah, while they are humbled} [al-Nahl: 48].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عَظْمَتِهِ وَسُلْطَانِهِ الَّذِي قَهَرَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَدَانَ لَهُ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ. وَلِهَذَا يسجُد لَهُ كُلُّ شَيْءٍ طَوْعًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَكَرْهَا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، ﴿وَظِلالُهُمْ بِالْغُدُوِّ﴾ أَيِ: البُكر وَالْآصَالِ، وَهُوَ جَمْعُ أَصِيلٍ وَهُوَ آخِرُ النَّهَارِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا إِلَى مَا خَلَقَ اللَّهُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ يَتَفَيَّأُ ظِلالُهُ عَنِ الْيَمِينِ وَالشَّمَائِلِ سُجَّدًا لِلَّهِ وَهُمْ دَاخِرُونَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٤٨] .

---

## 13:16 — verse 16

### Translation

He, Exalted, establishes that there is no god but Him, because they themselves acknowledge that He is the One who created the heavens and the earth, and that He is their Lord and Manager, yet despite this they have taken besides Him protectors whom they worship. Those gods possess no power for themselves, let alone for their worshippers, {of benefit or harm}, meaning they can neither obtain benefit nor repel harm. So can the one who worships these gods alongside Allah be equal to the one who worships Allah alone, with no partner, and who is upon light from his Lord? For this reason He said: {Say: Are the blind and the seeing equal? Or are darkness and light equal? Or have they attributed to Allah partners who created as He creates, so that creation became confused for them?} meaning: have these polytheists set up alongside Allah gods that rival the Lord and resemble Him in creating, such that they created as He creates, and creation became confused for them so that they cannot tell that it was created by another creator? That is: the matter is not so, for nothing resembles Him and nothing is His equal, He has no rival, no counterpart, no minister, no child and no consort. Exalted is Allah far above that, greatly exalted.

Rather, these polytheists worshipped alongside Him gods that they themselves acknowledged to be created by Him and to be His servants, just as they used to say in their talbiyah (pilgrim's invocation): "Here I am, You have no partner, except a partner who is Yours, You possess him and all that he possesses." This is as Allah, Exalted, reported of them in His saying: {We only worship them that they may bring us nearer to Allah} [al-Zumar: 3]. Allah, Exalted, rejected this from them, since they believed it, whereas He, Exalted, no one can intercede with Him except by His permission: {And intercession does not benefit with Him except for one whom He permits} [Saba: 23], {And how many an angel is there in the heavens whose intercession avails nothing except after Allah gives permission to whom He wills and is pleased with} [al-Najm: 26]. And He said: {There is none in the heavens and the earth but comes to the Most Merciful as a servant. He has enumerated them and counted them precisely, and each of them will come to Him on the Day of Resurrection alone} [Maryam: 93-95].

If all of them are servants, then why should some of them worship others without any evidence or proof, but merely by opinion, invention, and innovation? Then He sent His messengers, from the first of them to the last, restraining them from that and forbidding them from worshipping anyone besides Allah. But they denied them and opposed them, so the word of punishment was rightfully due upon them without doubt. {And your Lord wrongs no one} [al-Kahf: 49].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُقَرِّرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ مُعْتَرِفُونَ أَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ، وَهُوَ رَبُّهَا وَمُدَبِّرُهَا، وَهُمْ مَعَ هَذَا قَدِ اتَّخَذُوا مِنْ دُونِهِ أَوْلِيَاءَ يَعْبُدُونَهُمْ، وَأُولَئِكَ الْآلِهَةُ لَا تَمَلِكُ لِنَفْسِهَا وَلَا لِعَابِدِيهَا بِطَرِيقِ الْأَوْلَى ﴿نَفْعًا وَلا ضَرًّا﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُحَصِّلُ مَنْفَعَةً، وَلَا تَدْفَعُ مَضَرَّةً. فَهَلْ يَستَوي مَنْ عَبَدَ هَذِهِ الْآلِهَةَ مَعَ اللَّهِ، وَمِنْ عَبْدَ اللَّهَ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى نُورٍ مِنْ رَبِّهِ؟ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿قُلْ هَلْ يَسْتَوِي الأعْمَى وَالْبَصِيرُ أَمْ هَلْ تَسْتَوِي الظُّلُمَاتُ وَالنُّورُ أَمْ جَعَلُوا لِلَّهِ شُرَكَاءَ خَلَقُوا كَخَلْقِهِ فَتَشَابَهَ الْخَلْقُ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَجَعَلَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ مَعَ اللَّهِ آلِهَةً تُنَاظِرُ الرَّبَّ وَتُمَاثِلُهُ فِي الْخَلْقِ، فَخَلَقُوا كَخَلْقِهِ، فَتَشَابَهَ الْخَلْقُ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَلَا يَدْرُونَ أَنَّهَا مَخْلُوقَةٌ مِنْ مَخْلُوقٍ غَيْرِهِ؟ أَيْ: لَيْسَ الْأَمْرُ كَذَلِكَ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يُشَابِهُهُ شَيْءٌ وَلَا يُمَاثِلُهُ، وَلَا نِدَّ لَهُ وَلَا عدْل لَهُ، وَلَا وَزِيرَ لَهُ، وَلَا وَلَدَ وَلَا صَاحِبَةَ، تَعَالَى اللَّهُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ عُلُوًّا كَبِيرًا. وَإِنَّمَا عَبَدَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُشْرِكُونَ مَعَهُ آلِهَةً هُمْ يَعْتَرِفُونَ أَنَّهَا مَخْلُوقَةٌ لَهُ عَبِيدٌ لَهُ، كَمَا كَانُوا يَقُولُونَ فِي تَلْبِيَتِهِمْ: لَبَّيْكَ لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ، إِلَّا شَرِيكًا هُوَ لَكَ، تَمْلِكُهُ وَمَا مَلَكَ. وَكَمَا أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنْهُمْ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿مَا نَعْبُدُهُمْ إِلا لِيُقَرِّبُونَا إِلَى اللَّهِ زُلْفَى﴾ [الزُّمَرِ: ٣] فَأَنْكَرَ تَعَالَى ذَلِكَ عَلَيْهِمْ، حيث اعتقدوا ذلك، وهو تعالى لا يشفع عنده أحدإلا بِإِذْنِهِ، ﴿وَلا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا لِمَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ﴾ [سَبَأٍ: ٢٣] ، ﴿وَكَمْ مِنْ مَلَكٍ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ لَا تُغْنِي شَفَاعَتُهُمْ شَيْئًا إِلا مِنْ بَعْدِ أَنْ يَأْذَنَ اللَّهُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيَرْضَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٢٦] وَقَالَ: ﴿إِنْ كُلُّ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ إِلا آتِي الرَّحْمَنِ عَبْدًا لَقَدْ أَحْصَاهُمْ وَعَدَّهُمْ عَدًّا وَكُلُّهُمْ آتِيهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فَرْدًا﴾ [مَرْيَمَ: ٩٣ -٩٥] فَإِذَا كَانَ الْجَمِيعُ عَبِيدًا، فَلِمَ يَعْبُدُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا بِلَا دَلِيلٍ وَلَا بُرْهَانٍ، بَلْ بِمُجَرَّدِ الرَّأْيِ وَالِاخْتِرَاعِ وَالِابْتِدَاعِ؟ ثُمَّ قَدْ أَرْسَلَ رُسُلَهُ مِنْ أَوَّلِهِمْ إِلَى آخِرِهِمْ تَزْجُرُهُمْ عَنْ ذَلِكَ، وَتَنْهَاهُمْ عَنْ عِبَادَةِ مِنْ سِوَى اللَّهِ، فَكَذَّبُوهُمْ وَخَالَفُوهُمْ، فَحَقَّتْ عَلَيْهِمْ كَلِمَةُ الْعَذَابِ لَا مَحَالَةَ، ﴿وَلا يَظْلِمُ رَبُّكَ أَحَدًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٤٩] .

---

## 13:17 — verse 17

### Translation

This noble verse comprises two examples set forth: one for truth in its permanence and endurance, and one for falsehood in its dissipation and extinction. He, the Exalted, said: {He sends down water from the sky}, meaning rain, {and the valleys flow, each according to its measure}, meaning each valley takes according to its capacity. This one is large and holds a great deal of water, and this one is small and holds only according to its measure. This is a reference to hearts and their differing capacities: some of them can hold much knowledge, while others cannot accommodate much knowledge but rather fall short of it. {And the flood carries a rising foam}, meaning that upon the surface of the water flowing in these valleys there arises a foam that rises above it. This is one example.

Then His saying, {And from that which they heat in the fire}, this is the second example, namely what is smelted in fire, whether gold or silver, {seeking ornament}, meaning in order to make it into jewelry, or copper or iron, in order to make it into a useful article, for foam rises upon it just as foam rises upon the water.

{Thus does God set forth truth and falsehood}, meaning that when the two are brought together, falsehood has no permanence and no continuity, just as the foam does not remain with the water, nor with the gold and the like of what is smelted in the fire, but rather goes away and dissipates. Hence He said: {As for the foam, it passes away as scum}, meaning it is of no benefit, but rather scatters and is torn apart and goes off to the sides of the valley, clinging to the trees, and the winds scatter it. Likewise the dross of gold, silver, iron, and copper goes away, none of it returning, and nothing remains except the water, and that gold and the like, which is of benefit. Hence He said: {But as for that which benefits people, it remains in the earth. Thus does God set forth examples}, just as He, the Exalted, said: {And these examples We set forth for the people, but none understand them except those of knowledge} [al-Ankabut: 43].

One of the salaf (early generations) said: "Whenever I read an example in the Qur'an and did not understand it, I would weep for myself, because God, the Exalted, says: {And none understand them except those of knowledge}."

Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying, {He sends down water from the sky and the valleys flow, each according to its measure}: this is an example that God set forth. Hearts bear from it according to the measure of their certainty and their doubt. As for doubt, deeds are of no benefit with it, but as for certainty, God benefits its people through it. This is His saying, {As for the foam, it passes away as scum} [that is doubt], {but as for that which benefits people, it remains in the earth}, that is certainty. And just as jewelry is put into the fire, and its pure substance is taken while its dross is left in the fire, so too does God accept certainty and cast away doubt.

Al-Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas concerning His saying, {He sends down water from the sky and the valleys flow, each according to its measure, and the flood carries a rising foam}: he said, the flood carries what is in the valley of wood and refuse. {And from that which they heat in the fire}, that is gold, silver, ornament, useful articles, copper, and iron. Copper and iron have dross, and God made the example of their dross like the foam of the water. As for what benefits people, it is gold and silver, and as for what benefits the earth, it is what it has drunk of the water so that it produces growth. So He made that like righteous deeds, which remain for their doer, while evil deeds dissipate from their doer just as this foam goes away. Likewise guidance and truth come from God: whoever acts by the truth, it is his, and it remains just as what benefits people remains in the earth. Likewise iron: a knife or sword cannot be made from it until it is put into the fire, which consumes its dross, and its good part is extracted and put to use. Thus falsehood dissipates when the Day of Resurrection comes, when the people are made to stand and deeds are presented: falsehood swerves away and perishes, while the people of truth benefit from the truth.

Similar interpretations of this verse have been transmitted from Mujahid, al-Hasan al-Basri, Ata, Qatada, and more than one among the earlier and later generations.

God, glory be to Him and exalted is He, set forth for the hypocrites at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah two examples, one of fire and one of water. These are His saying, {Their example is like that of one who kindled a fire, and when it illuminated what was around him} [al-Baqarah: 17], the verse; then He said, {Or like a rainstorm from the sky in which there is darkness, thunder, and lightning} [al-Baqarah: 19], the verse.

Likewise He set forth for the disbelievers in Surat al-Nur two examples. One of them is His saying, {But those who disbelieve, their deeds are like a mirage in a lowland which the thirsty one supposes to be water} [al-Nur: 39], the verse. A mirage occurs only in intense heat. Hence it is reported in the two Sahihs: "It will be said to the Jews on the Day of Resurrection: What do you want? They will say: Our Lord, we are thirsty, give us to drink. It will be said: Will you not go down? So they will go down to the Fire, and behold, it will be like a mirage, parts of it crushing other parts."

Then He said in the other example, {Or like the darknesses in a vast, deep sea covered by waves, above which are waves, above which are clouds} [al-Nur: 40], the verse. And in the two Sahihs, from Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The example of the guidance and knowledge with which God has sent me is like that of abundant rain falling upon land. Part of it was good soil that absorbed the water and produced abundant herbage and pasture. Another part of it was hard ground that held the water, and God benefited people by it: they drank from it, gave water to their animals, and irrigated their crops. And another part of it fell on barren ground, which neither holds water nor produces herbage. That is the example of the one who understands the religion of God and benefits from what I was sent with, so that he learns and teaches, and the example of the one who does not raise his head to that at all, and does not accept the guidance of God with which I was sent."

This is a water-based example. And in another hadith, which Imam Ahmad reported:

[chain] Abd al-Razzaq told us, Ma'mar told us, from Hammam ibn Munabbih, who said: this is what Abu Hurayrah narrated to us from the Messenger of God ﷺ, that he said: "My example and your example is like that of a man who kindled a fire, and when it illuminated what was around him, moths and these creatures that fall into fire began to fall into it, and he began to hold them back, but they overpowered him and plunged into it." He said: "That is my example and your example: I take hold of your waists to keep you from the Fire, saying, come away from the Fire, come away from the Fire, but you overpower me and plunge into it." Both al-Bukhari and Muslim also related it in the two Sahihs. This is a fire-based example.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

اشْتَمَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ الْكَرِيمَةُ عَلَى مَثَلَيْنِ مَضْرُوبَيْنِ لِلْحَقِّ فِي ثَبَاتِهِ وَبَقَائِهِ، وَالْبَاطِلِ فِي اضْمِحْلَالِهِ وَفَنَائِهِ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَنزلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً﴾ أَيْ: مَطَرًا، ﴿فَسَالَتْ أَوْدِيَةٌ بِقَدَرِهَا﴾ أَيْ: أَخَذَ كُلُّ وَادٍ بِحَسْبِهِ، فَهَذَا كَبِيرٌ وَسِعَ كَثِيرًا مِنَ الْمَاءِ، وَهَذَا صَغِيرٌ فَوَسِعَ بِقَدْرِهِ، وَهُوَ إِشَارَةٌ إِلَى الْقُلُوبِ وَتَفَاوُتِهَا، فَمِنْهَا مَا يَسَعُ عِلْمًا كَثِيرًا، وَمِنْهَا مَا لَا يَتَّسِعُ لِكَثِيرٍ مِنَ الْعُلُومِ بَلْ يَضِيقُ عَنْهَا، ﴿فَاحْتَمَلَ السَّيْلُ زَبَدًا رَابِيًا﴾ أَيْ: فَجَاءَ عَلَى وَجْهِ الْمَاءِ الَّذِي سَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْأَوْدِيَةِ زَبَدٌ عَالٍ عَلَيْهِ، هَذَا مَثَلٌ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِمَّا يُوقِدُونَ عَلَيْهِ فِي النَّارِ﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الْمَثَلُ الثَّانِي، وَهُوَ مَا يُسْبَكُ فِي النَّارِ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ أَوْ فِضَّةٍ ﴿ابْتِغَاءَ حِلْيَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: لِيَجْعَلَ حِلْيَةً أَوْ نُحَاسًا أَوْ حَدِيدًا، فَيُجْعَلُ مَتَاعًا فَإِنَّهُ يَعْلُوهُ زَبَدٌ مِنْهُ، كَمَا يَعْلُو ذَلِكَ زَبَدٌ مِنْهُ. ﴿كَذَلِكَ يَضْرِبُ اللَّهُ الْحَقَّ وَالْبَاطِلَ﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا اجْتَمَعَا لَا ثَبَاتَ لِلْبَاطِلِ وَلَا دَوَامَ لَهُ، كَمَا أَنَّ الزَّبَدَ لَا يَثْبُتُ مَعَ الْمَاءِ، وَلَا مَعَ الذَّهَبِ وَنَحْوِهِ مِمَّا يُسْبَكَ فِي النَّارِ، بَلْ يَذْهَبُ وَيَضْمَحِلُّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَأَمَّا الزَّبَدُ فَيَذْهَبُ جُفَاءً﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ، بَلْ يَتَفَرَّقُ وَيَتَمَزَّقُ وَيَذْهَبُ فِي جَانِبَيِ الْوَادِي، وَيَعْلَقُ بِالشَّجَرِ وَتَنْسِفُهُ الرِّيَاحُ. وَكَذَلِكَ خَبَثُ الذَّهَبِ وَالْفِضَّةِ وَالْحَدِيدِ وَالنُّحَاسِ يَذْهَبُ، لَا يَرْجِعُ مِنْهُ شَيْءٌ، وَلَا يَبْقَى إِلَّا الْمَاءُ وَذَلِكَ الذَّهَبُ وَنَحْوُهُ يُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَمَّا مَا يَنْفَعُ النَّاسَ فَيَمْكُثُ فِي الأرْضِ كَذَلِكَ يَضْرِبُ اللَّهُ الأمْثَالَ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتِلْكَ الأمْثَالُ نَضْرِبُهَا لِلنَّاسِ وَمَا يَعْقِلُهَا إِلا الْعَالِمُونَ﴾ [الْعَنْكَبُوتِ: ٤٣] .

قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: كُنْتُ إِذَا قرأتُ مَثَلًا مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ فَلَمْ أَفْهَمْهُ بَكَيت عَلَى نَفْسِي؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَقُولُ: ﴿وَمَا يَعْقِلُهَا إِلا الْعَالِمُونَ﴾

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَنزلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً فَسَالَتْ أَوْدِيَةٌ بِقَدَرِهَا﴾

هَذَا مَثَلٌ ضَرَبَهُ اللَّهُ، احْتَمَلَتْ مِنْهُ الْقُلُوبُ عَلَى قَدْرِ يَقِينِهَا وَشَكِّهَا، فَأَمَّا الشَّكُّ فَلَا يَنْفَعُ مَعَهُ الْعَمَلُ، وَأَمَّا الْيَقِينُ فَيَنْفَعُ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَهْلَهُ. وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَمَّا الزَّبَدُ فَيَذْهَبُ جُفَاءً﴾ [وَهُوَ الشَّكُّ] ﴿وَأَمَّا مَا يَنْفَعُ النَّاسَ فَيَمْكُثُ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ وَهُوَ الْيَقِينُ، وَكَمَا يُجْعَلُ الْحُلِيُّ فِي النَّارِ فَيُؤْخَذُ خَالَصُهُ وَيُتْرَكُ خَبَثه فِي النَّارِ؛ فَكَذَلِكَ يَقْبَلُ اللَّهُ الْيَقِينَ وَيَتْرُكُ الشَّكَّ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَنزلَ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مَاءً فَسَالَتْ أَوْدِيَةٌ بِقَدَرِهَا فَاحْتَمَلَ السَّيْلُ زَبَدًا رَابِيًا﴾ يَقُولُ: احْتَمَلَ السَّيْلُ مَا فِي الْوَادِي مِنْ عُودٍ ودِمْنَة ﴿وَمِمَّا يُوقِدُونَ عَلَيْهِ فِي النَّارِ﴾ فَهُوَ الذَّهَبُ وَالْفِضَّةُ وَالْحِلْيَةُ وَالْمَتَاعُ وَالنُّحَاسُ وَالْحَدِيدُ، فَلِلنُّحَاسِ وَالْحَدِيدِ خَبَثٌ، فَجَعَلَ اللَّهُ مَثَلَ خَبَثِهِ كَزَبَدِ الْمَاءِ، فَأَمَّا مَا يَنْفَعُ النَّاسَ فَالذَّهَبُ وَالْفِضَّةُ، وَأَمَّا مَا يَنْفَعُ الْأَرْضَ فَمَا شَرِبَتْ مِنَ الْمَاءِ فَأَنْبَتَتْ. فَجَعَلَ ذَاكَ مِثْلَ الْعَمَلِ الصَّالِحِ يَبْقَى لِأَهْلِهِ، وَالْعَمَلِ السَّيِّئِ يَضْمَحِلُّ عَنْ أَهْلِهِ، كَمَا يَذْهَبُ هَذَا الزَّبَدُ، فَكَذَلِكَ الْهُدَى وَالْحَقُّ جَاءَا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ، فَمَنْ عَمِلَ بِالْحَقِّ كَانَ لَهُ، وَيَبْقَى كَمَا يَبْقَى مَا يَنْفَعُ النَّاسَ فِي الْأَرْضِ. وَكَذَلِكَ الْحَدِيدُ لَا يُسْتَطَاعُ أَنْ يُعْمَلَ مِنْهُ سِكِّينٌ وَلَا سَيْفٌ حَتَّى يُدْخَلَ فِي النَّارِ فَتَأْكُلُ خبَثَه، وَيُخْرَجُ جَيِّدُهُ فَيُنْتَفَعُ بِهِ. كَذَلِكَ يَضْمَحِلُّ الْبَاطِلُ إِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَأُقِيمَ النَّاسُ، وَعُرِضَتِ الْأَعْمَالُ، فَيَزِيغُ الْبَاطِلُ وَيَهْلَكُ، وَيَنْتَفِعُ أَهْلُ الْحَقِّ بِالْحَقِّ.

وَكَذَلِكَ رُوي فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ، وَعَطَاءٍ، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَغَيْرِ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ.

وَقَدْ ضَرَبَ اللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ لِلْمُنَافِقِينَ مَثَلَيْنِ نَارِيًّا وَمَائِيًّا، وَهُمَا قَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَثَلُهُمْ كَمَثَلِ الَّذِي اسْتَوْقَدَ نَارًا فَلَمَّا أَضَاءَتْ مَا حَوْلَهُ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٧] ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿أَوْ كَصَيِّبٍ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ فِيهِ ظُلُمَاتٌ وَرَعْدٌ وَبَرْقٌ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ١٩] . وَهَكَذَا ضَرَبَ لِلْكَافِرِينَ فِي سُورَةِ النُّورِ مَثَلَيْنِ، أَحَدُهُمَا: قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَعْمَالُهُمْ كَسَرَابٍ بِقِيعَةٍ يَحْسَبُهُ الظَّمْآنُ مَاءً﴾ [النُّورِ: ٣٩] الْآيَةَ، وَالسَّرَابُ إِنَّمَا يَكُونُ فِي شِدَّةِ الْحَرِّ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ: "فَيُقَالُ لِلْيَهُودِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: فَمَا تُرِيدُونَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: أيْ رَبَّنا، عَطِشْنَا فَاسْقِنَا. فَيُقَالُ: أَلَا تَرِدُونَ؟ فَيَرِدُونَ النَّارَ فَإِذَا هِيَ كَالسَّرَابِ يَحْطِم بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا".

ثُمَّ قَالَ فِي الْمَثَلِ الْآخَرِ: ﴿أَوْ كَظُلُمَاتٍ فِي بَحْرٍ لُجِّيٍّ يَغْشَاهُ مَوْجٌ مِنْ فَوْقِهِ مَوْجٌ مِنْ فَوْقِهِ سَحَابٌ﴾ الْآيَةَ [النُّورِ: ٤٠] . وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ مَثَلُ مَا بَعَثَنِي اللَّهُ بِهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالْعِلْمِ، كَمَثَلِ غَيْثٍ أَصَابَ أَرْضًا، فَكَانَ مِنْهَا طَائِفَةٌ قَبِلَتِ الْمَاءَ فَأَنْبَتَتِ الْكَلَأَ وَالْعُشْبَ الْكَثِيرَ، وَكَانَتْ مِنْهَا أَجَادِبَ أَمْسَكَتِ الْمَاءَ، فَنَفَعَ اللَّهُ بِهَا النَّاسَ، فَشَرِبُوا وَرَعَوْا وَسَقَوْا وَزَرَعُوا، وَأَصَابَتْ طَائِفَةً مِنْهَا [أُخْرَى] إِنَّمَا هِيَ قِيعَانٌ لَا تُمْسِكُ مَاءً وَلَا تُنْبِتُ كلأ فذلك مثل من فَقه فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ ونَفَعه اللَّهُ بِمَا بَعَثَنِي وَنَفَعَ بِهِ، فَعَلِم وَعَلَّم، وَمَثَلُ مَنْ لَمْ يَرْفَعْ بِذَلِكَ رَأْسًا وَلَمْ يَقْبَلْ هُدَى اللَّهِ الَّذِي أُرْسِلْتُ بِهِ". 

فَهَذَا مَثَلُ مَائِيٌّ، وَقَالَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ الذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ هَمَّامِ بْنِ مُنَبِّه قَالَ: هَذَا مَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "مَثَلِي وَمَثَلُكُمْ، كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ اسْتَوْقَدَ نَارًا، فَلَمَّا أَضَاءَتْ مَا حَوْلَهُ جَعَلَ الْفَرَاشُ وَهَذِهِ الدَّوَابُّ الَّتِي يَقَعْنَ فِي النَّارِ يَقَعْنَ فِيهَا، وَجَعَلَ يحجُزُهُنَّ وَيَغْلِبْنَهُ فَيَقْتَحِمْنَ فِيهَا". قَالَ: "فَذَلِكُمْ مَثَلِي وَمَثَلُكُمْ، أَنَا آخِذُ بحُجزكم عَنِ النَّارِ، هَلُمّ عَنِ النَّارِ [هَلُمّ عَنِ النَّارِ، هَلُمّ] فَتَغْلِبُونِي فَتَقْتَحِمُونَ فِيهَا". وَأَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَيْضًا فَهَذَا مَثَلٌ نَارِيٌّ.

---

## 13:18 — verse 18

### Translation

The Most High informs about the final outcome of the fortunate and the wretched, saying: {For those who respond to their Lord}, meaning: they obeyed Allah and His Messenger, submitted to His commands, and believed His reports of the past and the future, for them is {the best reward} which is the good recompense, as the Most High said, reporting concerning Dhu al-Qarnayn that he said: {He said, "As for one who wrongs, we will punish him. Then he will be returned to his Lord, and He will punish him with a terrible punishment. But as for one who believes and does righteousness, he will have the best reward, and we will speak to him from our command with ease"} [al-Kahf: 87, 88]. And the Most High said: {For those who have done good is the best reward and even more} [Yunus: 26].

His saying: {And those who did not respond to Him}, meaning: they did not obey Allah, {if they had all that is in the earth} meaning: in the Hereafter, if it were possible for them to ransom themselves from Allah's punishment with an earth full of gold and its like along with it, they would ransom themselves with it. But it would not be accepted from them, because the Most High will not accept from them on the Day of Resurrection any exchange or equivalent. {Those will have the worst reckoning}, meaning: in the Hereafter, that is, they will be called to account for the smallest speck and the thinnest membrane, for the great and the trivial, and whoever is called to strict account will be punished. Therefore He said: {And their refuge is Hell, and wretched is the resting place}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ مَآلِ السُّعَدَاءِ وَالْأَشْقِيَاءِ فَقَالَ: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَجَابُوا لِرَبِّهِمُ﴾ أَيْ: أَطَاعُوا اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ، وَانْقَادُوا لِأَوَامِرِهِ، وَصَدَّقُوا أَخْبَارَهُ الْمَاضِيَةَ وَالْآتِيَةَ، فَلَهُمُ ﴿الْحُسْنَى﴾ وَهُوَ الْجَزَاءُ الْحَسَنُ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ ذِي الْقَرْنَيْنِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: ﴿قَالَ أَمَّا مَنْ ظَلَمَ فَسَوْفَ نُعَذِّبُهُ ثُمَّ يُرَدُّ إِلَى رَبِّهِ فَيُعَذِّبُهُ عَذَابًا نُكْرًا وَأَمَّا مَنْ آمَنَ وَعَمِلَ صَالِحًا فَلَهُ جَزَاءً الْحُسْنَى وَسَنَقُولُ لَهُ مِنْ أَمْرِنَا يُسْرًا﴾ [الْكَهْفِ: ٨٧، ٨٨] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا الْحُسْنَى وَزِيَادَةٌ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٢٦] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ لَمْ يَسْتَجِيبُوا لَهُ﴾ أَيْ لَمْ: يُطِيعُوا اللَّهَ ﴿لَوْ أَنَّ لَهُمْ مَا فِي الأرْضِ جَمِيعًا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، لَوْ أَنْ يُمْكِنَهُمْ أَنْ يَفْتَدُوا مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ بِمَلْءِ الْأَرْضِ ذَهَبًا وَمِثْلَهُ مَعَهُ لَافْتَدَوْا بِهِ، وَلَكِنْ لَا يُتَقَبَّلُ مِنْهُمْ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى لَا يَقْبَلُ مِنْهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ صَرْفًا وَلَا عَدْلًا ﴿أُولَئِكَ لَهُمْ سُوءُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، أَيْ: يُنَاقَشُونَ عَلَى النَّقِيرِ وَالْقِطْمِيرِ، وَالْجَلِيلِ وَالْحَقِيرِ، وَمَنْ نُوقِشَ الْحِسَابَ عُذِّبَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَمَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ وَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ﴾

---

## 13:19 — verse 19

### Translation

The Almighty says: he who knows among mankind that what {has been sent down to you}, O Muhammad, {from your Lord} is {the truth}, that is, that which contains no doubt, no uncertainty, no confusion, and no contradiction, rather it is all truth confirming one part with another, no part of it opposing any other part, for its reports are all true and its commands and prohibitions are just, as the Almighty said: {And the word of your Lord has been completed in truthfulness and justice} [al-An'am: 115], meaning truthful in its reports and just in what it requires. So he who has verified the truth of what you have brought, O Muhammad, is not equal to one who is blind, who is not guided to good and does not understand it, and even if he understood it he would not submit to it, nor believe it, nor follow it. As the Almighty said: {The companions of the Fire and the companions of Paradise are not equal. The companions of Paradise are the ones who are successful} [al-Hashr: 20]. And He said in this noble verse: {Is he who knows that what has been sent down to you from your Lord is the truth like one who is blind?}, meaning: is this one like that one? There is no equivalence.

As for His saying, {Only those of understanding will remember}, meaning: only those possessed of sound, correct intellects take heed, reflect, and comprehend. May God make us among them, by His bounty and generosity.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: لَا يَسْتَوِي مَنْ يَعْلَمُ مِنَ النَّاسِ أَنَّ الَّذِي ﴿أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ﴾ يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿مِنْ رَبِّكَ﴾ هوَ ﴿الْحَقُّ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي لَا شَكَّ فِيهِ وَلَا مِرْيَةَ وَلَا لَبْسَ فِيهِ وَلَا اخْتِلَافَ فِيهِ، بَلْ هُوَ كُلُّهُ حَقٌّ يُصَدِّقُ بَعْضُهُ بَعْضًا، لَا يُضَادُّ شَيْءٌ مِنْهُ شَيْئًا آخَرَ، فَأَخْبَارُهُ كُلُّهَا حَقٌّ، وَأَوَامِرُهُ وَنَوَاهِيهِ عَدْلٌ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَتَمَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ صِدْقًا وَعَدْلا﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١١٥] أَيْ: صِدْقًا فِي الْأَخْبَارِ، وَعَدْلًا فِي الطَّلَبِ، فَلَا يَسْتَوِي مِنْ تَحَقَّقَ صِدْقَ مَا جِئْتَ بِهِ يَا مُحَمَّدُ، وَمَنْ هُوَ أَعْمَى لَا يَهْتَدِي إِلَى خَيْرٍ وَلَا يَفْهَمُهُ، وَلَوْ فَهِمَهُ مَا انْقَادَ لَهُ، وَلَا صَدَّقَهُ وَلَا اتَّبَعَهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا يَسْتَوِي أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ وَأَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ أَصْحَابُ الْجَنَّةِ هُمُ الْفَائِزُونَ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ: ٢٠] وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿أَفَمَنْ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّمَا أُنزلَ إِلَيْكَ مِنْ رَبِّكَ الْحَقُّ كَمَنْ هُوَ أَعْمَى﴾ أَيْ: أَفَهَذَا كَهَذَا؟ لَا اسْتِوَاءَ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا يَتَذَكَّرُ أُولُو الألْبَابِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا يَتَّعِظُ وَيَعْتَبِرُ وَيَعْقِلُ أُولُو الْعُقُولِ السَّلِيمَةِ الصَّحِيحَةِ جَعَلَنَا اللَّهُ مِنْهُمْ [بِفَضْلِهِ وَكَرَمِهِ] .

---

## 13:20-24 — verses 20-24 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Most High states, informing about those who are characterized by these praiseworthy qualities, that they will have {the good outcome of the abode}, which is the final result and support in this world and the next.

{Those who fulfill the covenant of Allah and do not break the pledge}, they are not like the hypocrites who, when one of them makes a covenant, betrays it, and when he disputes, he transgresses, and when he speaks, he lies, and when he is entrusted, he betrays.

{And those who join what Allah has commanded to be joined}, meaning the ties of kinship, and doing good to relatives, to the poor and needy, and giving generously. {And they fear their Lord}, that is, in what they do and what they refrain from doing among their deeds, they are watchful of Allah in that, and they fear the evil reckoning in the final abode. For this reason their affair is characterized by uprightness and steadfastness in all their movements and stillness, and in all their states, both those that concern themselves alone and those that concern others.

{And those who are patient seeking the countenance of their Lord}, meaning patient in refraining from forbidden things and sins, weaning their souls away from these things for the sake of Allah, Exalted and Glorified, seeking His good pleasure and His abundant reward. {And establish prayer} within its proper limits and set times, its bowing, prostration, and humility, in the manner prescribed by the Law and pleasing to Him. {And spend out of what We have provided for them}, meaning on those to whom spending is obligatory, such as wives, relatives, and others outside the family, among the poor, the needy, and those in want. {Secretly and openly}, that is, in private and in public, no circumstance whatsoever prevents them from this, in the hours of night and at the edges of day. {And they repel evil with good}, meaning they push away what is bad with what is good. So when someone wrongs them, they respond with what is fine, with patience, forbearance, pardon, and forgiveness, just as the Most High said: {Repel evil with that which is better, then the one between whom and you there was enmity will become as though he were a close friend. And none are granted this except those who are patient, and none are granted this except one of great fortune} [Fussilat: 34, 35].

For this reason He said, informing about these fortunate ones characterized by these good qualities, that they will have the good outcome of the abode. Then He explained that by saying: {Gardens of Eden}, and "Eden" (Adn) means permanent residence, that is, gardens of everlasting dwelling in which they will abide forever.

It is reported from Abdullah ibn Amr that he said: In Paradise there is a palace called "Eden," around which are towers and meadows. It has five thousand gates, and on each gate there are five thousand garments of fine cloth (hibarah). None enters it except a prophet, a truthful one (siddiq), or a martyr.

Al-Dahhak said regarding His words, {Gardens of Eden}: it is the city of Paradise, in which dwell the messengers, the prophets, the martyrs, and the leaders of guidance, with the people around them thereafter, and the gardens surrounding it. Both of these were narrated by Ibn Jarir.

As for His words, {And whoever among their fathers, spouses, and descendants was righteous}, meaning: they will be gathered together with their loved ones there, from among fathers, families, and children, among those among the believers who are fit to enter Paradise, so that their eyes may be delighted by them. Indeed, the rank of the lower one is raised up to the rank of the higher, without any diminishment to the higher one's rank, but rather as a favor and kindness from Allah, just as the Most High said: {And those who believed and whose descendants followed them in faith, We will join with them their descendants, and We will not deprive them of anything of their deeds. Every person is responsible for what he has earned} [al-Tur: 21].

As for His words, {And the angels will enter upon them from every gate, saying: Peace be upon you for what you patiently endured, and how excellent is the final abode}, meaning: the angels enter upon them from here and there to congratulate them on entering Paradise. So upon their entry into it, the angels come to them offering greetings and congratulating them for what they have attained from Allah of nearness, favor, and permanent residence in the abode of peace, in the company of the truthful ones, the prophets, and the noble messengers.

Imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Sa'id ibn Abi Ayyub told us, Ma'ruf ibn Suwayd al-Judhami told us, from Abu Ushanah al-Ma'afiri, from Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As, may Allah be pleased with them both, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Do you know who will be the first of Allah's creation to enter Paradise?" They said: "Allah and His Messenger know best." He said: "The first of Allah's creation to enter Paradise are the poor emigrants, by whom the frontier posts are secured and by whom hardships are warded off, and one of them dies with his need still in his breast, unable to fulfill it. So Allah, the Most High, says to whichever of His angels He wills: 'Go to them and greet them.' The angels say: 'We are the dwellers of Your heaven, and Your chosen ones among Your creation, yet You command us to go to these people and greet them?' He says: 'They were servants who worshipped Me, associating nothing with Me, and by them the frontier posts were secured and hardships were warded off, and one of them would die with his need still in his breast, unable to fulfill it.'" He said: "So the angels come to them at that point, entering upon them from every gate, {Peace be upon you for what you patiently endured, and how excellent is the final abode}."

Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani also narrated it, [chain] from Ahmad ibn Rishdin, from Ahmad ibn Salih, from Abdullah ibn Wahb, from Amr ibn al-Harith, from Abu Ushanah, who heard Abdullah ibn Amr, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "The first group to enter Paradise will be the poor emigrants, by whom hardships are warded off, who when commanded, hear and obey, and if one of them had a need directed toward a ruler, it would not be fulfilled until he died with it still in his breast. And Allah will call Paradise on the Day of Resurrection, and it will come with its splendor and adornment, and He will say: 'Where are My servants who fought in My cause, who were harmed in My cause, and who struggled in My cause? Enter Paradise without punishment and without reckoning.' And the angels will come and prostrate, saying: 'Our Lord, we glorify You night and day, and we sanctify You, who are these whom You have favored over us?' The Lord, Exalted and Glorified, will say: 'These are My servants who struggled in My cause and were harmed in My cause.' Then the angels will enter upon them from every gate: {Peace be upon you for what you patiently endured, and how excellent is the final abode}."

Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak said, [chain] from Baqiyyah ibn al-Walid, Artah ibn al-Mundhir told us, I heard a man from the elders of the army called "Abu al-Hajjaj" say: I sat with Abu Umamah and he said: The believer, when he enters Paradise, will be reclining on his couch, with two rows of servants around him, and at the end of the two rows there is a door with a gatekeeper. The angel comes and asks permission to enter, so [the farthest servant] says to the one next to him: "An angel is asking permission," and the one next to him says to the one next to him: "An angel is asking permission," until it reaches the believer, who says: "Let him in." Then the one closest to the believer says: "Let him in," and the one next to him says to the one next to him: "Let him in," until it reaches the farthest of them, who is at the door, and it is opened for him, and he enters, offers greetings, and then departs. Narrated by Ibn Jarir.

Ibn Abi Hatim also narrated it through the hadith of Ismail ibn Ayyash, from Artah ibn al-Mundhir, from Abu al-Hajjaj Yusuf al-Alhani, who said: I heard Abu Umamah, and he mentioned something similar.

It has come in the hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ used to visit the graves of the martyrs at the beginning of every year, and would say to them: {Peace be upon you for what you patiently endured, and how excellent is the final abode}. And likewise did Abu Bakr, Umar, and Uthman.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَمَّنِ اتَّصَفَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَمِيدَةِ، بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ ﴿عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ وَهِيَ الْعَاقِبَةُ وَالنُّصْرَةُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.

﴿الَّذِينَ يُوفُونَ بِعَهْدِ اللَّهِ وَلا يَنْقُضُونَ الْمِيثَاقَ﴾ وَلَيْسُوا كَالْمُنَافِقِينَ الَّذِينَ إِذَا عَاهَدَ أَحَدُهُمْ غَدَرَ، وَإِذَا خَاصَمَ فَجَرَ، وَإِذَا حَدَّثَ كَذَبَ، وَإِذَا ائْتُمِنَ خَانَ.

﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَصِلُونَ مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَنْ يُوصَلَ﴾ مِنْ صِلَةِ الْأَرْحَامِ، وَالْإِحْسَانِ إِلَيْهِمْ وَإِلَى الْفُقَرَاءِ وَالْمَحَاوِيجِ، وَبَذْلِ الْمَعْرُوفِ، ﴿وَيَخْشَوْنَ رَبَّهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا يَأْتُونَ وَمَا يَذْرُوَنَ مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ، يُرَاقِبُونَ اللَّهَ فِي ذَلِكَ، وَيَخَافُونَ سُوءَ الْحِسَابِ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ. فَلِهَذَا أَمْرُهُمْ عَلَى السَّدَادِ وَالِاسْتِقَامَةِ فِي جَمِيعِ حَرَكَاتِهِمْ وَسَكَنَاتِهِمْ وَجَمِيعِ أَحْوَالِهِمُ الْقَاصِرَةِ وَالْمُتَعَدِّيَةِ.

﴿وَالَّذِينَ صَبَرُوا ابْتِغَاءَ وَجْهِ رَبِّهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: عَنِ الْمَحَارِمِ وَالْمَآثِمِ، فَفَطَمُوا نُفُوسَهُمْ عَنْ ذَلِكَ لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ؛ ابْتِغَاءَ مَرْضَاتِهِ وَجَزِيلِ ثَوَابِهِ ﴿وَأَقَامُوا الصَّلاةَ﴾ بِحُدُودِهَا وَمَوَاقِيتِهَا وَرُكُوعِهَا وَسُجُودِهَا وَخُشُوعِهَا عَلَى الْوَجْهِ الشَّرْعِيِّ الْمَرْضِي، ﴿وَأَنْفَقُوا مِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى الَّذِينَ يَجِبُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْإِنْفَاقُ لَهُمْ مِنْ زَوْجَاتٍ وَقَرَابَاتٍ وَأَجَانِبَ، مِنْ فُقَرَاءَ وَمَحَاوِيجَ وَمَسَاكِينَ، ﴿سِرًّا وَعَلانِيَةً﴾ أَيْ: فِي السِّرِّ وَالْجَهْرِ، لَمْ يَمْنَعْهُمْ مِنْ ذَلِكَ حَالٌ مِنَ الْأَحْوَالِ، فِي آنَاءِ اللَّيْلِ وَأَطْرَافِ النَّهَارِ، ﴿وَيَدْرَءُونَ بِالْحَسَنَةِ السَّيِّئَةَ﴾ أَيْ: يَدْفَعُونَ الْقَبِيحَ بِالْحَسَنِ، فَإِذَا آذَاهُمْ أَحَدٌ قَابَلُوهُ بِالْجَمِيلِ صَبْرًا وَاحْتِمَالًا وَصَفْحًا وَعَفْوًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ادْفَعْ بِالَّتِي هِيَ أَحْسَنُ فَإِذَا الَّذِي بَيْنَكَ وَبَيْنَهُ عَدَاوَةٌ كَأَنَّهُ وَلِيٌّ حَمِيمٌ وَمَا يُلَقَّاهَا إِلا الَّذِينَ صَبَرُوا وَمَا يُلَقَّاهَا إِلا ذُو حَظٍّ عَظِيمٍ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٣٤، ٣٥] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ مُخْبِرًا عَنْ هَؤُلَاءِ السُّعَدَاءِ الْمُتَّصِفِينَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَسَنَةِ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ، ثُمَّ فَسَّرَ ذَلِكَ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ﴾ وَالْعَدْنُ: الْإِقَامَةُ، أَيْ: جَنَّاتُ إِقَامَةٍ يَخْلُدُونَ فِيهَا.

وَعَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو أَنَّهُ قَالَ: إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ قَصْرًا يُقَالُ لَهُ: "عَدْنٌ"، حَوْلَهُ الْبُرُوجُ وَالْمُرُوجُ، فِيهِ خَمْسَةُ آلَافِ بَابٍ، عَلَى كُلِّ بَابٍ خَمْسَةُ آلَافِ حِبْرة لَا يَدْخُلُهُ إِلَّا نَبِيٌّ أَوْ صِدِّيقٌ أَوْ شَهِيدٌ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ﴾ مَدِينَةُ الْجَنَّةِ، فِيهَا الرُّسُلُ وَالْأَنْبِيَاءُ وَالشُّهَدَاءُ وَأَئِمَّةُ الْهُدَى، وَالنَّاسُ حَوْلَهُمْ بَعْدُ وَالْجَنَّاتُ حَوْلَهَا. رَوَاهُمَا ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَنْ صَلَحَ مِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَأَزْوَاجِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: يُجْمَعُ بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ أَحْبَابِهِمْ فِيهَا مِنَ الْآبَاءِ وَالْأَهْلِينَ وَالْأَبْنَاءِ، مِمَّنْ هُوَ صَالِحٌ لِدُخُولِ الْجَنَّةِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ؛ لِتَقَرَّ أَعْيُنُهُمْ بِهِمْ، حَتَّى إِنَّهُ تُرْفَعُ دَرَجَةُ الْأَدْنَى إِلَى دَرَجَةِ الْأَعْلَى، مِنْ غَيْرِ تَنْقِيصٍ لِذَلِكَ الْأَعْلَى عَنْ دَرَجَتِهِ، بَلِ امْتِنَانًا مِنَ اللَّهِ وَإِحْسَانًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَاتَّبَعَتْهُمْ ذُرِّيَّتُهُمْ بِإِيمَانٍ أَلْحَقْنَا بِهِمْ ذُرِّيَّتَهُمْ وَمَا أَلَتْنَاهُمْ مِنْ عَمَلِهِمْ مِنْ شِيْءٍ كُلُّ امْرِئٍ بِمَا كَسَبَ رَهِينٌ﴾ [الطَّوْرِ: ٢١] . 

وَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالْمَلائِكَةُ يَدْخُلُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ كُلِّ بَابٍ سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَا صَبَرْتُمْ فَنِعْمَ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: وَتَدْخُلُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ مِنْ هَاهُنَا وَهَاهُنَا لِلتَّهْنِئَةِ بِدُخُولِ الْجَنَّةِ، فَعِنْدَ دُخُولِهِمْ إِيَّاهَا تَفِدُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ مُسَلِّمِينَ مُهَنِّئِينَ لَهُمْ بِمَا حَصَلَ لَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنَ التَّقْرِيبِ وَالْإِنْعَامِ، وَالْإِقَامَةِ فِي دَارِ السَّلَامِ، فِي جِوَارِ الصِّدِّيقِينِ وَالْأَنْبِيَاءِ وَالرُّسُلِ الْكِرَامِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنِي سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي أَيُّوبَ، حَدَّثَنَا مَعْرُوفُ بْنُ سُوَيْد الْجُذَامِيُّ عَنْ أَبِي عُشَّانَةَ الْمَعَافِرِيِّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ أَوَّلَ مَنْ يَدْخُلُ الْجَنَّةَ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ؟ " قَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "أَوَّلُ مَنْ يَدْخُلُ الْجَنَّةَ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ الْفُقَرَاءُ المهاجرون الذين تُسدُّ بهم الثغور، وتُتَّقَى بِهِمُ الْمَكَارِهُ، وَيَمُوتُ أَحَدُهُمْ وَحَاجَتُهُ فِي صَدْرِهِ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ لَهَا قَضَاءً، فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ مَلَائِكَتِهِ: ائْتُوهُمْ فَحَيُّوهُمْ. فَتَقُولُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ: نَحْنُ سُكَّانُ سَمَائِكَ، وَخِيرَتُكَ مَنْ خَلْقِكَ، أَفَتَأْمُرُنَا أَنْ نَأْتِيَ هَؤُلَاءِ فَنُسَلِّمَ عَلَيْهِمْ؟ قَالَ: إِنَّهُمْ كَانُوا عِبَادًا يَعْبُدُونَنِي لَا يُشْرِكُونَ بِي شَيْئًا، وتُسَد بِهِمُ الثُّغُورُ، وَتُتَّقَى بِهِمُ الْمَكَارِهُ، وَيَمُوتُ أَحَدُهُمْ وَحَاجَتُهُ فِي صَدْرِهِ فَلَا يَسْتَطِيعُ لَهَا قَضَاءً". قَالَ: "فَتَأْتِيهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ، فَيَدْخُلُونَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ كُلِّ بَابٍ، ﴿سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَا صَبَرْتُمْ فَنِعْمَ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ 

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ رِشْدِينَ، عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ عَمْرو بْنِ الْحَارِثِ، عَنْ أَبِي عُشَّانة سَمِعَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قال: "أَوَّلُ ثُلَّةٍ يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ فُقَرَاءُ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ، الَّذِينَ تُتَّقَى بِهِمُ الْمَكَارِهُ، وَإِذَا أُمِرُوا سَمِعُوا وَأَطَاعُوا، وَإِنْ كَانَتْ لِرَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ حَاجَةٌ إِلَى سُلْطَانٍ لَمْ تُقْضَ حَتَّى يَمُوتَ وَهِيَ فِي صَدْرِهِ، وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَدْعُو يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ الْجَنَّةَ فَتَأْتِي بِزُخْرُفِهَا وَزِينَتِهَا، فَيَقُولُ: أَيْنَ عِبَادِي الَّذِينَ قَاتَلُوا فِي سَبِيلِي، وَأُوذُوا فِي سَبِيلِي، وَجَاهَدُوا فِي سَبِيلِي؟ ادْخُلُوا الْجَنَّةَ بِغَيْرِ عَذَابٍ وَلَا حِسَابٍ، وَتَأْتِي الْمَلَائِكَةُ فَيَسْجُدُونَ وَيَقُولُونَ: رَبَّنَا نَحْنُ نُسَبِّحُكَ اللَّيْلَ وَالنَّهَارَ، ونُقدس لَكَ، مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ آثَرْتَهُمْ عَلَيْنَا؟ فَيَقُولُ الرَّبُّ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: هَؤُلَاءِ عِبَادِي الَّذِينَ جَاهَدُوا فِي سَبِيلِي، وَأُوذُوا فِي سَبِيلِي فَتَدْخُلُ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ مِنْ كُلِّ بَابٍ: ﴿سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَا صَبَرْتُمْ فَنِعْمَ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ بَقِيَّة بْنَ الْوَلِيدِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَرْطَاةُ بْنُ الْمُنْذِرِ، سَمِعْتُ رَجُلًا مِنْ مَشْيَخَةِ الْجُنْدِ، يُقَالُ لَهُ "أَبُو الْحَجَّاجِ" يَقُولُ: جَلَسْتُ إِلَى أَبِي أُمَامَةَ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنَ لَيَكُونُ مُتَّكِئًا عَلَى أَرِيكَتِهِ إِذَا دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ، وَعِنْدَهُ سِمَاطَانِ مِنْ خَدَمٍ، وَعِنْدَ طَرَفِ السِّمَاطَيْنِ بَابٌ مُبَوَّبٌ، فَيُقْبِلُ الْمَلَكُ فَيَسْتَأْذِنُ، فَيَقُولُ [أَقْصَى الْخَدَمِ] لِلَّذِي يَلِيهِ: "مَلك يَسْتَأْذِنُ"، وَيَقُولُ الَّذِي يَلِيهِ لِلَّذِي يَلِيهِ: "مَلَكٌ يَسْتَأْذِنُ"، حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ الْمُؤْمِنَ فَيَقُولُ: ائْذَنُوا. فَيَقُولُ أَقْرَبُهُمْ إِلَى الْمُؤْمِنِ: ائْذَنُوا، وَيَقُولُ الَّذِي يَلِيهِ لِلَّذِي يَلِيهِ: ائْذَنُوا حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ أَقْصَاهُمُ الَّذِي عِنْدَ الْبَابِ، فَيَفْتَحُ لَهُ، فَيَدْخُلُ فَيُسَلِّمُ ثُمَّ يَنْصَرِفُ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. 

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، عَنْ أَرْطَاةَ بن المنذر، عن أبي الحجاج يُوسُفَ الْأَلْهَانِيِّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا أُمَامَةَ، فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ.

وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَزُورُ قُبُورَ الشُّهَدَاءِ فِي رَأْسِ كُلِّ حَوْلٍ، فَيَقُولُ لَهُمْ: ﴿سَلامٌ عَلَيْكُمْ بِمَا صَبَرْتُمْ فَنِعْمَ عُقْبَى الدَّارِ﴾ وَكَذَا أَبُو بَكْرٍ، وَعُمَرُ وَعُثْمَانُ.

---

## 13:25 — verse 25

### Translation

This is the state of the wretched ones and their characteristics. He then mentioned their end in the Hereafter and their destination, which is opposite to what the believers arrive at, just as they were characterized by attributes opposite to theirs in this world. For those believers used to fulfill God's covenant and join what God commanded to be joined, while these {break God's covenant after it has been contracted, and sever what God has commanded to be joined, and spread corruption in the earth}, as is established in the hadith: "The sign of the hypocrite is three: when he speaks he lies, when he promises he breaks his promise, and when he is entrusted he betrays the trust." And in another version: "and when he makes a pact he is treacherous, and when he disputes he transgresses."

Therefore He said: {those, for them is the curse}, meaning being cast far away from mercy, {and for them is the evil of the abode}, meaning an evil end and outcome, and their refuge is Hell, and what an evil resting place it is.

Abu al-Aliyah said regarding His statement, {those who break God's covenant}, the verse: this refers to six traits found in the hypocrites. When they have the upper hand over people, they display these traits: when they speak they lie, when they promise they break their promise, when they are entrusted they betray the trust, they break God's covenant after it has been contracted, they sever what God has commanded to be joined, and they spread corruption in the earth. But when the upper hand is against them, they display only the three traits: when they speak they lie, when they promise they break their promise, and when they are entrusted they betray the trust.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا حَالُ الْأَشْقِيَاءِ وَصِفَاتُهُمْ، وَذَكَرَ مَآلَهُمْ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ وَمَصِيرَهُمْ إِلَى خِلَافِ مَا صَارَ إِلَيْهِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ، كَمَا أَنَّهُمُ اتَّصَفُوا بِخِلَافِ صِفَاتِهِمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَأُولَئِكَ كَانُوا يُوفُونَ بِعَهْدِ اللَّهِ وَيَصِلُونَ مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَنْ يُوصَلَ، وَهَؤُلَاءِ ﴿يَنْقُضُونَ عَهْدَ اللَّهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مِيثَاقِهِ وَيَقْطَعُونَ مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَنْ يُوصَلَ وَيُفْسِدُونَ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "آيَةُ الْمُنَافِقِ ثَلَاثٌ: إِذَا حَدَّثَ كَذَبَ، وَإِذَا وَعَدَ أَخْلَفَ، وَإِذَا اؤْتُمِنَ خَانَ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "وَإِذَا عَاهَدَ غَدَرَ، وَإِذَا خَاصَمَ فَجر".

وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ لَهُمُ اللَّعْنَةُ﴾ وَهِيَ الْإِبْعَادُ عَنِ الرَّحْمَةِ، ﴿وَلَهُمْ سُوءُ الدَّارِ﴾ وَهِيَ سُوءُ الْعَاقِبَةِ وَالْمَآلِ، وَمَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ وَبِئْسَ الْقَرَارُ. 

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَنْقُضُونَ عَهْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: هِيَ سِتُّ خِصَالٍ فِي الْمُنَافِقِينَ إِذَا كَانَ فِيهِمُ الظَّهرة عَلَى النَّاسِ أَظْهَرُوا هَذِهِ الْخِصَالَ: إِذَا حَدَّثُوا كَذَبُوا، وَإِذَا وَعَدُوا أَخْلَفُوا، وَإِذَا ائْتُمِنُوا خَانُوا، وَنَقَضُوا عَهْدَ اللَّهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مِيثَاقِهِ، وَقَطَعُوا مَا أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ أَنْ يُوصَلَ، وَأَفْسَدُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ. وَإِذَا كَانَتِ الظَّهرة عَلَيْهِمْ أَظْهَرُوا الثَّلَاثَ الْخِصَالَ: إِذَا حَدَّثُوا كَذَبُوا، وَإِذَا وَعَدُوا أَخْلَفُوا، وَإِذَا ائْتُمِنُوا خَانُوا.

---

## 13:26 — verse 26

### Translation

The Almighty mentions that He is the One who expands provision for whomever He wills and restricts it for whomever He wills, because of the wisdom and justice that He has in that. These disbelievers rejoiced in what they were given in the worldly life, as a gradual luring (istidraj) of them and a granting of respite, as the Almighty said: {Do they think that what We extend to them of wealth and children, We hasten to them good things? Rather, they do not perceive} [al-Mu'minun: 55, 56].

Then He belittled the worldly life in relation to what He, the Almighty, has stored up for His believing servants in the Abode of the Hereafter, saying: {And the worldly life compared to the Hereafter is nothing but a passing enjoyment}

Just as He said: {Say: the enjoyment of this world is little, and the Hereafter is better for one who fears Allah, and you will not be wronged even by a thread} [al-Nisa: 77], and He said: {Rather, you prefer the worldly life, while the Hereafter is better and more lasting} [al-A'la: 16, 17].

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] al-Mustawrid, brother of Banu Fihr, said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "The worldly life compared to the Hereafter is nothing but like what one of you would find if he put this finger of his into the sea, so let him see with what it returns," and he pointed with his index finger. Muslim related it in his Sahih.

In another hadith: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ passed by a dead kid goat with small ears (al-asakk means small-eared), and he said, "By Allah, the worldly life is more insignificant to Allah than this is to its owners when they threw it away."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي يُوَسِّعُ الرِّزْقَ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَيُقَتِّرُهُ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ، لِمَا لَهُ فِي ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْحِكْمَةِ وَالْعَدْلِ. وَفَرِحَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْكُفَّارِ بِمَا أُوتُوا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا اسْتِدْرَاجًا لَهُمْ وَإِمْهَالًا كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَيَحْسَبُونَ أَنَّمَا نُمِدُّهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ مَالٍ وَبَنِينَ نُسَارِعُ لَهُمْ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ بَل لَا يَشْعُرُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ٥٥، ٥٦] .

ثُمَّ حَقَّرَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا بِالنِّسْبَةِ إِلَى مَا ادَّخَرَهُ تَعَالَى لِعِبَادِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا فِي الآخِرَةِ إِلا مَتَاعٌ﴾

كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿قُلْ مَتَاعُ الدُّنْيَا قَلِيلٌ وَالآخِرَةُ خَيْرٌ لِمَنِ اتَّقَى وَلا تُظْلَمُونَ فَتِيلا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٧٧] وَقَالَ ﴿بَلْ تُؤْثِرُونَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةُ خَيْرٌ وَأَبْقَى﴾ [الْأَعْلَى: ١٦، ١٧] .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع وَيَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ أَبِي خَالِدٍ، عَنْ قَيْسٍ، عَنِ الْمُسْتَوْرِدِ أَخِي بَني فِهْرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا الدُّنْيَا فِي الْآخِرَةِ إِلَّا كَمَثَلِ مَا يَجْعَلُ أَحَدُكُمْ إِصْبَعَهُ هَذِهِ فِي الْيَمِّ، فَلْيَنْظُرْ بِمَ تَرْجِعُ" وَأَشَارَ بِالسَّبَّابَةِ. وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ. 

وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم مَرَّ بِجَدْيٍ أسكَّ ميتٍ -وَالْأَسَكُّ الصَّغِيرُ الْأُذُنَيْنِ -فَقَالَ: "وَاللَّهِ لِلدُّنْيَا أَهْوَنُ عَلَى اللَّهِ مِنْ هَذَا عَلَى أَهْلِهِ حِينَ أَلْقَوْهُ".

---

## 13:27-29 — verses 27-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about what the polytheists said: {Why not} that is, why not {a sign was not sent down to him from his Lord} just as they said: {Let him bring us a sign as the earlier ones were sent} [al-Anbiya: 5]. Discussion of this has already occurred more than once, and indeed God is capable of answering what they asked. It is reported in a hadith that God revealed to His Messenger, when they asked him to turn al-Safa into gold for them, to make a spring flow for them, and to remove the mountains around Mecca so that meadows and orchards would take their place: "If you wish, O Muhammad, I will give them that, and if they then disbelieve I will punish them with a punishment I have not inflicted on anyone in the worlds. But if you wish, I will open for them the gate of repentance and mercy." He said, "Rather, open for them the gate of repentance and mercy." For this reason He said to His Messenger: {Say, indeed God leads astray whom He wills and guides to Himself whoever turns to Him in repentance}, meaning: He is the One who leads astray and the One who guides, whether He sends the Messenger with a sign matching what they proposed or does not answer their request. Guidance and misguidance are not tied to that or its absence, just as He said: {And of what benefit are signs and warnings to a people who do not believe} [Yunus: 101], and He said: {Indeed, those against whom your Lord's word has been justified will not believe even if every sign came to them, until they see the painful punishment} [Yunus: 96-97], and He said: {And even if We had sent down to them the angels, and the dead had spoken to them, and We had gathered together before them every kind of thing, they would not have believed unless God willed, but most of them are ignorant} [al-An'am: 111]. For this reason He said: {Say, indeed God leads astray whom He wills and guides to Himself whoever turns to Him in repentance}, meaning: He guides whoever turns to God, returns to Him, seeks His help, and humbles himself before Him.

{Those who believe and whose hearts find rest in the remembrance of God}, meaning: their hearts become good and incline toward God's side, find tranquility at the mention of Him, and are content with Him as protector and helper. For this reason He said: {Truly, it is in the remembrance of God that hearts find rest}, meaning: He is truly deserving of that.

{Those who believe and do righteous deeds, tuba is for them and a good place of return.} Ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas: joy and delight of the eye. Ikrimah said: excellent is their possession. Al-Dahhak said: it is a state to be envied for them. Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said: it is good for them.

Qatadah said: it is an Arabic expression, a man says "tuba laka," meaning: you have attained good. And in another report he said: {tuba lahum} means goodness is for them.

{And a good place of return} means: a good place to which one comes back.

These sayings are all one thing, with no contradiction among them.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr reported from Ibn Abbas: {tuba lahum}, he said: it is the land of Paradise in the Abyssinian language.

Sa'id ibn Masjuh said: tuba is the name of Paradise in the Indian language. Likewise al-Suddi reported from Ikrimah: {tuba lahum} meaning: Paradise. Mujahid said the same.

Al-'Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas: when God created Paradise and finished creating it, He said: {Those who believe and do righteous deeds, tuba is for them and a good place of return}, and that was when it pleased Him.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Shahr ibn Hawshab said: {tuba} is a tree in Paradise, and every tree of Paradise comes from it, its branches extending beyond the wall of Paradise.

Similarly it has been reported from Abu Hurayrah, Ibn Abbas, Mughith ibn Sumayy, Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i, and more than one of the early scholars, that tuba is a tree in Paradise, and in every dwelling of Paradise there is a branch of it.

Some of them mentioned that the Merciful, blessed and exalted is He, planted it with His own hand from a single pearl seed, and commanded it to extend, and it extended to wherever God, blessed and exalted is He, willed, and from its root sprang the springs of the rivers of Paradise, of honey, wine, water, and milk.

Abdullah ibn Wahb said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may God be pleased with him, [raised report: "Tuba is a tree in Paradise whose extent is a hundred years' journey; the garments of the people of Paradise come forth from its sheaths."] And Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, from the Messenger of God ﷺ: that a man said, "O Messenger of God, tuba for whoever sees you and believes in you." He said, "Tuba for whoever sees me and believes in me, then tuba, then tuba, then tuba for whoever believes in me without seeing me." A man said to him, "What is tuba?" He said, "A tree in Paradise whose extent is a hundred years; the garments of the people of Paradise come forth from its sheaths."

Al-Bukhari and Muslim both reported, [chain] from Sahl ibn Sa'd, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "In Paradise there is a tree in whose shade a rider travels for a hundred years without crossing it." He said: I related this to al-Nu'man ibn Abi Ayyash al-Zuraqi, and he said: Abu Sa'id al-Khudri related to me, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "In Paradise there is a tree in whose shade a rider on a swift, well-trained racing steed travels a hundred years without crossing it."

In Sahih al-Bukhari, from the hadith of Yazid ibn Zuray', from Sa'id, from Qatadah, from Anas, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said concerning God's saying {and extended shade} [al-Waqi'ah: 30]: "In Paradise there is a tree in whose shade a rider travels for a hundred years without crossing it."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "In Paradise there is a tree in whose shade a rider travels a hundred years. Recite, if you wish, {and extended shade}." Both [al-Bukhari and Muslim] reported it in their Sahihs.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] I heard Abu al-Dahhak relating from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "In Paradise there is a tree in whose shade a rider travels seventy, or a hundred, years; it is the tree of eternity."

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: [chain] from Asma bint Abi Bakr, may God be pleased with her, who said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ, and he mentioned the Lote Tree of the utmost boundary (Sidrat al-Muntaha), and said: "A rider travels in the shade of a single branch of it for a hundred years, or he said: a hundred riders take shade in a single branch of it. In it are cushions of gold, as though its fruit were water jars." Reported by al-Tirmidhi.

Isma'il ibn Ayyash said: [chain] from Abu Umamah al-Bahili, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "There is none of you who enters Paradise but he is taken to tuba, and its sheaths are opened for him, and he takes from it whatever he wishes: if he wishes white, or if he wishes red, or if he wishes yellow, or if he wishes black, like the anemone flower (shaqa'iq al-nu'man) but finer and more beautiful."

Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: tuba is a tree in Paradise; God says to it, "Open up for My servant whatever he wishes," so it opens for him horses with their saddles and bridles, camels with their halters, and whatever clothing he wishes.

Ibn Jarir also reported from Wahb ibn Munabbih here a strange and remarkable report (gharib, unusual report). Wahb, may God have mercy on him, said: in Paradise there is a tree called "tuba," in whose shade a rider travels a hundred years without crossing it. Its blossoms are fine striped cloth, its leaves are garments, its twigs are ambergris, its ground is ruby, its soil is camphor, and its mud is musk. From its root flow rivers of wine, milk, and honey. It is a gathering place for the people of Paradise. While they are sitting together, angels come to them from their Lord leading swift she-camels bridled with chains of gold, their faces like lamps in beauty, their fur like the softest fine wool in its softness. On them are saddles whose sides are of ruby, whose panels are of gold, and whose coverings are of fine silk (sundus) and brocade (istabraq). They make them kneel and say: "Our Lord has sent us to you so that you may visit Him and greet Him with peace." He said: so they mount them, and they are swifter than birds and softer than cushions, moving in intimate conversation without any effort, a man riding alongside his brother while conversing and speaking privately with him. No ear of one mount touches the ear of another, nor does the kneeling place of one mount touch that of another, so much so that a tree will move aside from their path so as not to separate a man from his brother.

He said: They will come to the Most Merciful, the Most Compassionate, and He will unveil His noble Face to them until they gaze upon Him. When they see Him, they will say: "O Allah, You are al-Salam (the Source of Peace) and from You comes peace, and to You belongs majesty and honor." He said: Allah, exalted is He, will then say: "I am al-Salam and from Me comes peace, and upon you My mercy and My love have become due. Welcome, O My servants who feared Me in the unseen and obeyed My command."

He said: They will say: "Our Lord, we did not worship You as You deserve to be worshipped, nor did we esteem You as You deserve to be esteemed. So grant us permission to prostrate before You." He said: Allah will say: "This is not a house of toil or worship, but a house of dominion and bliss. I have lifted from you the toil of worship, so ask Me whatever you wish, for every man among you has his desire." So they will ask Him, until even the one among them whose desire is shortest will say: "My Lord, the people of the world competed fiercely over their world and were straitened by it. My Lord, grant me the like of everything they possessed from the day You created it until the world came to an end." Allah, exalted is He, will say: "Your desire has indeed fallen short, and you have asked for less than your true station. This is yours from Me, and I shall also honor you with a gift befitting My station, for there is no stinginess or curtailment in My giving."

He said: Then He will say: "Show My servants what has not reached their desires and has not even occurred to their minds." He said: So it will be shown to them until their own desires, which were in their hearts, seem paltry by comparison. Among what will be shown to them will be paired steeds, upon every four of which is a couch made from a single ruby, upon every couch of which is a dome of hollow-cast gold, in every dome of which are layered beds from the beds of Paradise, in every dome of which are two maidens of the wide-eyed houris, upon each of whom are two garments from the garments of Paradise. There is no color in Paradise but is found in these two garments, and no fragrant scent but has permeated them. The light of their faces penetrates the thickness of the dome, so that whoever sees them would think they were outside the dome rather than within it. One can see the marrow of their legs through their shins, like a white thread within a red ruby. Each of them appears to the other, in terms of excellence, like the excellence of the sun over stones, or even greater, and he too will appear to them in the same way. He enters unto them, and they greet him, kiss him, and embrace him, saying to him: "By Allah, we never imagined that Allah could create anyone like you." Then Allah, exalted is He, will command the angels, and they will lead them in ranks through Paradise, until each man among them is brought to the station that has been prepared for him.

Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this report with his chain, from Wahb ibn Munabbih, and he added: "So look at the gift of your Lord which He has bestowed upon you." And behold, there are domes in al-Rafiq al-A'la (the Highest Companionship), and chambers built of pearl and coral, whose doors are of gold, whose couches are of ruby, whose furnishings are of fine silk and brocade, and whose pulpits are of light. Light gushes forth from their doors and courtyards like the radiance of the sun, compared to which the shining star appears as in the brightness of day.
